Data-driven AI (e.g， machine learning) achieves tremendous success over the past decade in achieving human-competitive performance in many cutting-edge domains. Recently， we also have also been witnessing an increasing trend of new AI technique proposals in the cy ber-physical systems across industrial domains， e.g，autonomous driving， robotics， power and energy， especially in solving problems that could not be achieved by classical solutions (e.g， theory and best practice) under open， wild， or extreme conditions. In general， for a complex CPS，AI components can be deployed as one or multiple as its key components for prediction， analysis， optimization and control tasks. In this talk， I would give a high-level introduction to some of our ongoing activities towards addressing the trustworthy challenges of AI-enabled cyber-physical systems， and highlight a few future directions that we have recently started towards building and ensuring the safety and reliability of the AI-enabled cyber-physical systems in the data-driven era.

李丽华，女，1966年11月生，汉族，中共党员，研究生学历，法学硕士，毕业于西南政法学院刑事诉讼法专业，历任深圳市人民检察院检委办副主任、案件管理处副处长，深圳市福田区人民检察院党组成员、副检察长，深圳市光明区人民检察院党组书记、检察长等职务，现任深圳市南山区人民检察院党组书记、检察长、南山区委政法委副书记。
Dark matter (DM) comprises approximately 27% of :the energy in the observable universe. Unveiling the properties of DM is one of the most important tasks in modern. physics. Benefiting from the rapid developments of the precision frontier， especially through the. techniques of quantum sensing， it has become possible to probe large unexp lored parameterspace of dark matter. Among DM candidates， dark photon dark matter is particularly promising. I will first demonstrate how to utilize a resonant (LC-circuit) and a broad-band (SERF) electromagnetic detector to search for the kinetically mixed dark photon DM. Both proposals are already realized， and promising. results are delivered. In addition， a gravitational wave detector (LIGO) or an optomechanical system can also be used to efficiently search for the U(1)_{B-L} dark photon DM. The results from these two methods deliver the. world records in certain parameter space.
Natural products with complex chemical structures are important sources of drugs， which have long challenged the capability of human beings to create molecules. Total synthesis of natural products constitutes one of the most challenging and influential fundamental research in the field of organic chemistry. Notably， it provides a vital basis for ensuring the supply of natural medicines with structural diversity. This presentation includes two aspects of contents. First， aiming to address the key issue of efficient construction of natural product skeletons， we have achieved the total syntheses of an array of indole alkaloids and diterpenoid alkaloids bearing most intricate structures， by developing target-oriented innovative synthetic methods and strategies. Second， driven by the demands on drugs in the field of life health， we have accomplished the asymmetric industrial total syntheses of three complex natural medicines with breakthrough of the existing bottleneck， by raising and solving the essential scientific problems in natural product synthesis.
Two-dimensional (2D) strongly correlated electrons remains one of central themes in modern physics. In this talk， we address a crucial issue: whether there exists a paradigm to study 2D strongly correlated electrons， starting from its one- dimensional reduction? We will demonstrate that newly proposed Gutzwiller projected wavefunction guided density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) is a promising method on this theme. This method is illustrated by several examples: (1) The benchmark on the famous Kitaev honeycomb model; (2) Unveiling a nematic spin-orbital liquid ground state on the simplest spin-orbital model on the simplest frustrated lattice; (3) Attacking a challenging problem: what is the ground state of the antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model on a Kagome lattice?
单细胞测序技术对免疫细胞的功能状态识别与干预策略研发产生了根本性的影响，尤其使得我们有能力对肿瘤免疫中的众多核心问题进行全新的解析。我们利用生物信息学方法和单细胞组学技术，深度研究了多种实体瘤中肿瘤浸润免疫细胞的功能状态，并在跨癌种水平上进行了系统性的比较，进而以此为基础，揭示了肿瘤患者免疫治疗响应差异的分子机制。另外，我们分析了非小细胞肺癌和三阴乳腺癌在接受免疫治疗过程中的浸润性免疫细胞动态变化，发现了在有效和无效病人中的基线区别，也发现了治疗过程中变化最显著的免疫细胞亚型。在前期泛癌种T细胞和髓系细胞的基础上，B细胞，NK细胞，和成纤维细胞，鉴定了更多和肿瘤微环境相关的细胞亚型以及它们的具体特征。最终，我们初步发现了肿瘤微环境的整体特征和临床特征的相关性。这对肿瘤免疫的新靶点的发现、以及和临床预后相关的生物标记物的鉴定提供了前瞻性的基础。
近年来，使用光学传感原理的微流控免疫传感技术快速发展。相比传统免疫分析技术，新一代免疫传感技术的灵敏度大幅度提高，动态范围显著增大，所需样本量进一步减小。一些原先被认为难以分析的宝贵生物标本逐渐成为了新型生物分子信息的宝库。基于化学发光、微腔激光等新型光学传感原理，我们开发了-系列光微流生物分子免疫传感技术。我们将其中稳定性最好、灵敏度优异的的自动化化学发光ELISA技术被功应用在了小鼠血清/尿液肿瘤标记物定量分析、外泌体膜蛋白表达谱分析等生命科学研究中。2020年新冠肺炎疫情爆发后，基于这一技术平台，我们也将其应用于快速筛查高lgG丰度康复期血清捐献者和重组抗体/纳米抗体的体外性能评估工作中。在本次报告中，除讨论微流控化学发光免疫分析技术之外，我也将介绍激光发射显微成像技术(LEM)的原理和进展。
When alphas are weak and rare， and arbitrageurs have to learn about alphas from historical data，there is a gap between Sharpe ratio that is feasible for them to achieve and the infeasible Sharpe ratio that could be obtained with perfect knowledge of parameters in the return generating process. This statistical limit to arbitrage widens the bounds within which alphas can survive in equilibrium relative to the arbitrage pricing theory (APT) in which arbitrageurs are endowed with perfect knowledge. We derive the optimal Sharpe ratio achievable by any feasible arbitrage strategy， and ilustrate in a simple model how this Sharpe ratio varies with the strength and sparsity of alpha signals， which characterize the difficulty of arbitrageurs' learning problem.Furthermore， we design an all-weather" arbitrage strategy that achieves this optimal Sharpe ratio regardless of the conditions of alpha signals. Our empirical analysis of equity returns shows that this optimal strategy， along with other feasible strategies based on multiple- testing， LAsSO， and Ridge methods， achieve a moderately low Sharpe ratio out of sample， in spite of a considerably higher infeasible Sharpe ratio， consistent with absence of feasible near-arbitrage opportunities and relevance of statistical limits to arbitrage.
This talk will give an overview of Nature journals and the editorial process involved in publishing. The discussions will especially include what editors do， what they look for， and how they make decisions， together with some practical tips for writing and submitting a paper to a Nature journal.
B细胞、浆细胞介导的体液免疫是帮助人体抵御病原体入侵的关键机制之一。针对包括新冠病毒、流感病毒等不断突变的病原体，如何能够促进人体产生持久、广谱的兔疫反应仍是我们]亟需解决地难题。报告人将以一系列针对新冠病毒的研究为例，介绍如何利用分子生物学技术及大数据分析手段，精准地表征人体中具有不同抗原特异性的免疫反应及免疫记忆特征，并揭示B细胞相关的抗原特异性免疫记忆在不同组织和不同人群中的分布规律。
Heterogeneous catalysis has been a key focus for researchers across many disciplines，including chemistry， physics， materials science and even engineering and to understand the subject is one of the ultimate goals in physical science. In the last twenty years or so， theoretical catalysis has become very important to achieve this goal. In this talk， firstly I will briefly review the history of theoretical catalysis. Then， | will present some of recent theoretical progresses in heterogeneous catalysts. I will show how photo-catalytic progresses can be simulated using DFT. The adsorption/ desorption in catalytic processes will be discussed.
As a carrier and participant， surface and interface provide special environments for supramolecular chemistry and on-surface chemical reactions， enabling real-space and high-resolution imaging as well. Supramolecular chemistry is the study on ordered molecular structures formed by self- assembly based on weak interactions such as hydrogen bonds， van der Waals forces， and metal. organic coordination.On-surface chemistry investigates the construction of macromolecules and polymers prepared onsurfaces with well-defined structures through intermolecular or intramolecular reactions. Single crystal surfaces provide unique platforms for the regulation of chemical reactions， especially the selective control of reactions through the inherent characteristics of two-dimensional and one-dimensional spatial confinement and different adsorption sites. The obtained molecular structures are featured of designability， which is conducive to the construction and realization of special functional molecular structures which are difficult to produce with traditional chemistry.
产甲烷古菌是地球早期的生命形式之一，是研究生命起源与进化的代表性物种;产甲烷古菌是有机质庆氧降解产甲烷过程中的功能微生物是大气甲烷排放的主要贡献者，在全球碳循环过程中发挥重要作用。产甲烷古菌也是地下深部生物圈，如生物成因天然气形成的主要参与者最近几年，基于高通量测序的未培养组技术，预测了丰富多样的产甲烷古菌种群和代谢多样性潜力。报告人结合课题组的工作，介绍非广古菌门古菌，以及降解煤炭和原油产甲烷古菌的研究进展，并探讨它们在地下深部圈，特别是油藏和煤层的生物地球化学功能。
EIT cooling is a fast cooling method. for removing the .motional energy. of a large number of trapped ions. However， for a large number of ions， this method shows less efficiency due to its limited cooling bandwidth. In this talk， I will introduce a parallel-EIT cooling method， which has unlimited cooling bandwidth theoretically. Experimentally we demonstrate a cooling bandwidth over 5 MHz and cooling of all motional modes of a 4-ion string; In the second part， I will talk about the progress for quantum structural phase transition in trapped ion system. we realize the quantum version of the linear-zigzag structural transition for arrays of up to five ground state cooled ions held in a linear Paul trap and we demonstrate several of the control requirements towards entangled-state interferometry near the critical point. Using in-situ spectroscopy we probe the energy level structure and occupation of the soft mode associated with the structural transition， and show a stable critical point and majority ground state occupation crossing the transition.
本报告主要介绍团队在量子点发光材料与器件、自驱动纳米传感器、铜基薄膜光伏电池等方面的研究工作。
Big data is typically characterized with 4V's: Volume， Velocity， Variety and Veracity. When it comes to big graphs， these challenges become even more staggering. A number of questions remain open， from theory to systems and practice. Is it possible to parallelize single-machine algorithms and guarantee the correctness of the parallelized computations? What parallel computation model should we adopt to scale with big graphs? Is there a systematic method for developing effective incremental algorithms in response to frequent updates? Is it possible to uniformly query relational databases and semistructured graphs by using SQL? How can we unify logic rules and machine learning models， to improve the quality of graph-structured data， deduce associations between entities， and interpret event predictions? This talk aims to incite interest in these topics. It raises as many questions as it answers.

Swept lasers are the key components in laser frequency scanning interferometers which are widely applied in spectral detection systems including optical frequency domain reflectometer， swept source optical coherence tomography， optical sensing， and LiDAR. High sweep rate， wide sweep range， and long coherence length are the most desirable features of swept lasers.This talk will introduce broadband， highly stable and coherent swept lasers including Fourier domain mode locked lasers and time stretched swept lasers. The characterization techniques for swept lasers and their applications in biomedical imaging， high resolution measurement will also be presented.
希波克拉底誓词针对的是行业医生，强调服务、不伤害、尊重隐私等。近现代相关伦理扩展到医学和更广泛的科技领域。现代“技科”系统的运作展现出新的特点，从选题、立项、研发，再到发表、应用，整个链条都涉及伦理问题，事后评估为时已晚。现代社会，技科能人的智力活动影响深远。股市预测、地震预报、软件设计、人体增强、人工智能都内在地包含不同形式的伦理问题。在资本、权力与技科的互相支撑下，行为人的责任界定起来非常麻烦。技科系统的风险覆盖要包括个体、团体、国家、生物多样性、地球盖娅的健康等，既有短期也有长远影响，这对从业者提出更严格的要求，入职业需要进行类似希氏誓词的宣誓。

细胞外基质中的胶原蛋白为几乎所有的人体组织提供机械支撑和生化环境。胶原蛋白的特征性的分子结构一一三螺旋，在疾病和损伤中可能会被损坏和变性。为了探测胶原蛋白的损伤，我们提出并验证了胶原蛋白杂交的概念:模仿胶原蛋白的肽链可能与天然胶原蛋白的变性链形成杂交的三螺旋，而不是完整的三螺旋胶原蛋白，从而能够评估疾病组织内可能的胶原降解或机械破坏情况。本次汇报将描述胶原杂交的概念和发展，总结了我们对胶原三螺旋折叠规则的化学基础的拓展，讨论越来越多的生物医学证据，表明胶原的变性是涉及病理组织重塑和机械损伤的一系列组织细胞外基质的新特征。最后，我们希望与各位探讨有关胶原变性的化学、力学和生物医学的新问题，以及靶向的诊疗的新机会。
This paper investigates the problem of matrix completion from corrupted data， when additional covariates are available. Despite being seldomly considered in the matrix completion literature， these covariates often provide valuable information for completing the unobserved entries of the high-dimensional target matrix $A$. Given a covariate matrix $X$ with its rows representing the row covariates of $A$， we consider a column-space-decomposition model $A=X \beta+B$ where $Ibeta$ is a coefficient matrix and $B$ is a low-rank matrix orthogonal to $X$ in terms of column space.This model facilitates a clear separation between the interpretable covariate effects and the flexible hidden factor effects. Besides， our work allows the probabilities of observation to depend on the covariate matrix， and hence a missing-at-random mechanism is permitted. We propose anovel penalized estimator for $A$ by utilizing both Frobenius-norm and nuclear-norm regularizations with an efficient and scalable algorithm. Asymptotic convergence rates of the proposed estimators are studied. The empirical performance of the proposed methodology is illustrated via both numerical experiments and a real data application.
报告从中国应对新冠病毒感染疫情这一全球公共危机的策略出发，阐述总体国家安全观体系下的中国生物安全观，介绍生物安全危机的演进与历史沿革，对《生物安全法》、《病原微生 物实验室生物安全管理条例》等生物安全相关法律法规和技术标准的要点内容进行讲解，并结合实验室获得性感染实例分享病原微生物实验室风险评估方法及生物安全管理体系建设与运行经验，呼吁培育“生物安全与负责任行为”的文化，提出构建更强大的公共卫生体系、提升生物安全治理能力的建议。
Eukaryotic mRNA typically contains the 7-methylguanosine cap (the m7G cap)， which not only protects mRNAs from degradation but also plays an essential role in other steps of RNA metabolism and function， such as pre-mRNA processing and translation initiation. m7G capping was once considered to be a constitutive housekeeping process; however， growing evidence indicates that it is dynamically regulated in response to stimuli. In recent years， some RNAs in both prokaryotes and eukaryotes were found to contain non-canonical caps， such as the NAD cap， indicating another layer of control of gene expression by RNA capping. We have developed multiple methods for global-scale profiling of NAD-capped RNAS (NAD- RNAs). In those methods， NAD-RNAS are tagged by an enzymatic reaction and click chemistry. Labelled NAD-RNAS can then be enriched to make a library and identified by a 2nd or 3rd generation sequencing technology. Our recent data from NAD-RNA profiling of various organisms， including Arabidopsis and micro-organisms， will be presented. In plants， we have found that the Arabidopsis NAD-RNA decapping enzyme DX01 is also an essential component of m7G capping.DXO1 binds to and activate RNMT1 which methylates the guanosine cap of pre-mRNA to form the m7G cap. The finding indicates a novel mechanism in m7G capping in plants by coupling with decapping of NAD-RNA. Studies of the emerging NAD-RNA biology could elucidate novel mechanisms controlling important biological processes， such as organisms' responses to environmental stimuli.
Concept drift is known as an unforeseeable change in underlying streaming data distribution over time. The phenomenon of concept drift has been recognized as the root cause of decreased effectiveness in many decision-related applications. A promising solution for coping with persistent environmental change and avoiding system performance degradation is to build a detection and adaptive system. This talk will present a set of methods and algorithms that can effectively and accurately detect， understand， and adapt concept drift. The main contents include (1)competence models to indirectly measure variations in data distribution through changes in competence. By detecting changes in competence，differences in data ditribution can be accurately detected and quantified， then further described in unstructured data streams; (2) algorithms for determining a drift region to identify when and where a concept drift takes place in a data stream， and a local drift degree measurement that can continuously monitor regional density changes; (3) methods for concept drift adaptation. The new algorithms and techniques can be applied to data-driven prediction and rcal-time decision support in complex rcal-world environments.
受体相互作用丝氨酸/苏氨酸蛋白激酶 1 (RIPK1)是NF-κB促存活信号和细胞死亡信号转导的关键调控因子，以响应在人类疾病发生过程中广泛存在的炎症和促死亡刺激。RIPK1的激活促进细胞死亡和炎症。在人类疾病的动物模型中，抑制RIPK1可有效控制疾病进程，显示出了明显疗效。在自身免疫病和神经退行性疾病的人类尸检病理标本中也证实了RIPK1的激活。RIPK1变构调控结构域中有一个独特的疏水性口袋，可以作为抑制其激酶活性的高选择性小分子药物开发靶点，在临床前模型和人类临床试验中已对其安全性进行了验证。这些RIPK1抑制剂越来越多应用于治疗单基因和多基因自身免疫病、炎症、神经退行性疾病、缺血和急性疾病（例如重症新冠肺炎败血症）等多种疾病。在此，我们将探讨RIPK1生物学特性，RIPK1信号通路中与疾病相关的突变，特别是基础研究如何向人类疾病治疗方案进行转化。

This talk is focused on the development of bifunctional phosphines that are based amino acid structural motifs. Such phosphine catalysts can be readily prepared， very stable and structurally highly tunable， and their applications to a broad range of enantioselective organic reactions will be presented. The research context leading to the evolution of amino acid-based phosphines and some future research perspectives will also be outlined.
Unlike fellow non-segmented negative- strand RNA viruses， exemplified by the devastating Ebola， rabies， and measles viruses， vesicular stomatitis virus (VSV) can be considered beneficial， as it is widely used as a vector for anticancer therapy and vaccine development. The genome of VSV encodes 5 proteins in the following order: N (nucleoprotein)， P (phosphoprotein)， M (matrix protein)， G (glycoprotein) and L (large polymerase). AlI of these proteins are present in the mature， infectious virions. Lack of in situ atomic structures of these viral components has limited mechanistic understanding of assembling the bullet-shaped virion. Here， we have used cryo-electron tomography (cryoET) to visualize the VSV virion， revealing the attachment of the ring-shaped L to N throughout the cavity of the bullet-shaped nucleocapsid. Subtomogram averaging and three-dimensional classification of regions containing N and the M have yielded the in situ structure of the polymerase complex. On average， ~55 polymerase complexes are packaged in each virion. Further， we have determined the in situ structures of M and N at 3.47 A resolution by cryo-electron microscopy (cryoEM) and sub-particle reconstruction. In the virion， Nand M sites have a stoichiometry of 1:2. N-RNA， N-N， and N-M-M interactions govern the formation of the capsid. The pseudo-crystalline organization of G is further mapped by cryoET. The mechanism of VSV assembly is delineated by the network interactions of these viral components.
针对电动汽车车载充电系统容量不断增大、快速充电及可靠性要求不断提高等新需求，以提高车载充电系统经济性能和可靠性为目标，提出并研究了一类具有大功率及高可靠性特征的电动汽车用多相永磁电驱重构型车载充电(EDROC)系统。本课题针对该类EDROC系统的工作原理、充电过程中绕组通电对永磁电机损耗、电感及电磁转矩等电磁特性的影响、网侧模块并联控制及容错控制等基础问题开展研究工作，在拓扑设计与分析、电磁分析、目标优化控制、样机研制等四个方面取得了突破性进展。
Life is an exergonic chemical reaction. In the search for life's origin， the microbiologist wants to know: What was the chemical reaction from which the first cells arose， and what was the chemical reaction that fuelled the first free living cells? These are questions about chemistry and physiology， but molecular evolution can contribute. The last universal common ancestor (LUCA) is the assemblage of cells from which all life evolved roughly four billion years ago. Genomes and phylogeny have yielded new avenues to understanding early evolution and LUCA that had the universal genetic code shared by all descendant life forms. But how did LUCA harness energy? From the standpoint of CO2 fixation， the acetyl-CoA pathway is clearly the most ancient energy harnessing form. Organisms that use the acetyl CoA pathway from carbon and energy metabolism generate their ion gradient from the reduction of CO2 with H2 and harness energy from the process of CO2 fixation. Using data from sequenced microbial genomes， we reconstructed the physiology of LUCA by asking which genes trace to LUCA by phylogenetic criteria. We found that LUCA lived from gases - H2， CO2， H2S， co， N2 - in a setting that looked very much like a modern submarine hydrothermal vent.The results indicate that the first forms of life were anaerobic chemoautotrophs that evolved from preexisting geochemical processes involving exergonic reactions of H2， metals， and CO2.
Studying and understanding the surface and interfacial electrochemical processes with higher sensitivity，higher spatial and temporal resolution is a grand challenge in the field of in-situ electrochemical characterization. We establish electrochemical microscope based on surface -enhanced Raman spectroscopy to reveal the local electrochemical activity on electrode surfaces and develop high-sensitivity in-situ electrochemical dark-field spectroscopy that uncovers the electrodeposition process on single nanoparticle surface. Utilizing tip-enhanced Raman spectroscopy， we reveal the size effect of catalysts， and establish the correlation between surface structure， electronic and catalytic properties of catalysts at single-particle level.Lastly， I will introduce the development of electrochemical tip enhanced Raman spectroscopy and its application on studying the evolution of the structure and activity of electrocatalysts at nanometer scale.
We consider distributed statistical optimization and inference in the presence of heterogeneity among distributed data blocks. A weighted distributed estimator is proposed to improve the statistical efficiency of the standard "split-and-conquer" estimator for the common parameter shared by all the data blocks. The weighted distributed estimator is at least as efficient as the would-be full sample and the generalized method of moment estimators with the latter two estimators requiring full data access. A bias reduction is formulated for the weighted distributed estimator to accommodate much larger numbers of data blocks than the existing methods without sacrificing the statistical efficiency at the same time. The mean square error bounds， the asymptotic distributions， and the corresponding statistical inference procedures of the weighted distributed and the debiased estimators are derived， which shows an advantageous performance of the debiased weighted estimators when the number of data blocks is large.
在数字再现-虚拟推演现实交互的数字李生架构下，介绍从真实世界到虚拟世界的城市广域建筑基本信息的高效获取方法、考虑建筑-区域双尺度交互的城市抗震韧性过程数字推演方法和虚实交互的建筑室内人员地震安全混合现实演练方法，建立城市建筑地震情景，揭示其地震韧性特征，服务城市防灾规划与安全应急演练，为提升城市建筑抗震韧性提供了数字孪生解决方案。
人为什么 会得肿瘤?为什么不同的人得了同样的肿瘤会有不同的预后?为什么有些人很难得肿瘤?这些问题，使用传统的生物医学手段很难研究，因为肿瘤发生、发展、转移的真实环境很难在实验室模拟。随着生物技术的发展，肿瘤学者现在可以从患者身上切下来的肿瘤组织中获得大量的信息，包括基因组、转录组、代谢组数据，通称为组学大数据。这些组织包括不同发展阶段的肿瘤，甚至癌前期的组织。这给学者们提供了-个研究从正常细胞到晚期肿瘤演化的绝好机会。弄懂肿瘤的演化过程，需要懂一点进化理论。具体地，当体内器官的化学环境发生了改变，将给相关的细胞造成生存压力，这将转化为细胞内的氧化压力，它会导致DNA突变，有些突变会被选择来克服或适应压力。那发生肿瘤的组织受到哪些压力呢?通过一系列的计算化学分析， 我们发现:(i)肿瘤中发生变化的绝大多数代谢过程有一个共同点: 它们都比相应的正常代谢方式产生更多的氢离子(酸性)。我们还发现:所有发生肿瘤的器官中都有慢性炎症及铁积累，这两者的结合将不断产生氢氧根(碱性)。进一步的计算表明:每个肿瘤组织中代谢所产生氢离子的速度与慢性发炎结合铁积累产生氢氧根的速度高度一致。已有的知识告诉我们:细胞内的pH需要高度稳定，否则就会死。因而我们推测:当慢性发炎开始改变细胞的pH时，为存活，细胞改变了一系列的代谢方式，以产生足够的氢离子，以维持细胞的pH稳定，使细胞能活下来。而这些改变了的代谢方式造成了一系列的细胞新行为，包括(1)持续的细胞增殖、 (2)细胞转移、 (3)细胞耐药等。我将简单地介绍如何使用"系统生物学”方法，来研究肿瘤各种行为(临床表现)。这一框架的建立，使得肿瘤研究变得更大众化。我在佐治亚大学的实验室一直有本科生做原创性的研究，如在过去20年，年轻人患肠癌的个数大幅增加的原因及机理。我们的研究是通过大数据分析来解各种各样的”迷”。如果你有兴趣，请加入我们。
人体主要由人体细胞和人体微生物(Human Microbiome)组成，其中人体微生物的种类( ~ 300- 500种/每人)，数量(~1014个/每人)和基因总数(> 100万/每人)超过人体细胞。对于人体微生物对宿主生理和病理活动的调控作用以及分子机制，有待深入研究。陈海威博士(1) 利用功能性筛选体系(PRESTO- Tango) ，揭示了人体微生物可以分泌活性小分子代谢物，通过靶向宿主的G蛋白偶联受体(GPCR) ，来调控宿主多种生理活动(Chen et al.， Cell，2019) ; (2)开发新型的功能性高通量筛选体系(PRESTO-Salsa) ，初步系统性绘制人体/人体微生物代谢物GPCR作用图谱(Chen et al， Cell， under revision;PCT/US2019/065226; https://palmlab shinyapps.io/presto salsa/)。这两项研究成果，为系统性研究人体微生物的功能和分子机制，提供了新的科研思路研究方法。
When alphas are weak and rare， and arbitrageurs have to learn about alphas from historical data，there is a gap between Sharpe ratio that is feasible for them to achieve and the infeasible Sharpe ratio that could be obtained with perfect knowledge of parameters in the return generating process. This statistical limit to arbitrage widens the bounds within which alphas can survive in equilibrium relative to the arbitrage pricing theory (APT) in which arbitrageurs are endowed with perfect knowledge. We derive the optimal Sharpe ratio achievable by any feasible arbitrage strategy， and ilustrate in a simple model how this Sharpe ratio varies with the strength and sparsity of alpha signals， which characterize the difficulty of arbitrageurs' s learning problem. Furthermore， we design an“ ll-weather" arbitrage strategy that achieves this optimal Sharpe ratio regardless of the conditions of alpha signals. Our empirical analysis of equity returns shows that this optimal strategy， along with other feasible strategies based on multiple-testing， LASSO， and Ridge methods， achieve a moderately low Sharpe ratio out of sample， in spite of a considerably higher infeasible Sharpe ratio， consistent with absence of feasible near-arbitrage opportunities and relevance of statistical limits to arbitrage.
神经运动控制是基于脑、脊髓与肌肉的层级式结构，由运动命令神经信号和感觉反馈神经信号构成的闭环动力学系统。研究神经在感觉运动闭环系统中的控制机制是神经科学的重要问题，同时也为脑机接口的应用提供了科学理论基础。即便机械系统与神经运动系统在控制载体的具体形式上有诸多不同，但是基于机械系统运动控制的本质思想，并与动力学、人工智能、控制理论等学科相结合，对于研究神经运动控制的动力学本质具有重要意义。本次学术报告围绕神经感觉运动控制闭环系统，主要对四个方面展开探讨: (1) 基于神经网络以及贝叶斯估计方法的神经感觉反馈状态估计问题; (2) 局部振动诱发本体感觉神经信号与脊髓反射调控肌张力的作用机制; (3) 以猕猴为动物模型，通过侵入式电极阵列与循环神经网络计算模型研究运动与感觉皮层群体神经元对于肢体运动的控制机制，主要面向的神经科学问题为脑与脊髓反射对于运动任务的协同控制机制、神经状态空间内的运动规划与运动解码、以及冗余控制任务的感觉运动皮层协同控制机制; (4) 最后，通过行为学实验证明脑可以通过子运动达成对复杂动力学系统的运动任务控制。
Biostatistics is the interdisciplinary science of mathematics and biomedicine， and is the application of mathematics and statistics in the fields of biology， public health and medicine. In this talk， I will introduce the important role of biostatistics in biology， medicine and public health. I will also review the history of the development of biostatistics. Finally， 1 will discuss some of my methodologic work in three areas of biostatistics: (1) causal inference， (2) diagnostic medicine， and (3) infectious disease epidemiology.
Non-Markovian models of stochastic biochemical kinetics often incorporate explicit time delays to effectively model large numbers of intermediate biochemical processes. Analysis and simulation of these models， as well as the inference of their parameters from data， are fraught with difficulties because the dynamics depends on the system' S history. Here we use an artificial neural network to approximate the time- dependent distributions of non- Markovian models by the solutions of much simpler time-inhomogeneous Markovian models; the approximation does not increase the dimensionality of the model and simultaneously leads to inference of the kinetic parameters. The training of the neural network uses a relatively small set of noisy measurements generated by experimental data or stochastic simulations of the non-Markovian model. We show using a variety of models， where the delays stem from transcriptional processes and feedback control， that the Markovian models learnt by the neural network accurately reflect the stochastic dynamics across parameter space.
In the noisy intermediate-scale quantum era (NISQ)， we are likely to achieve practicat quantum advantage using near-term programmable quantum hardware. To further develop the understanding of NISQ， we made progresses in three aspects: quantum algorithms， quantum simulation， and quantum software. In this talk， I will discuss how to apply quantum-neural hybrid scheme [1， 2] and quantim architecture search [3， 4] to design variational quantum algorithms and apply quantum error mitigation. I will also discuss how to use quantum computer to model and simulate novel non-equilibrium quantum states and dynamics [5， 6]. Finally; I will introduce the .high-performance quantum software.framework for the NISQ era一TensorCircuit [7]: These works together pave the way to better understand and investigate the power of NISQ devices.
拓扑物理的发现是凝聚态体系和经典波系统的重要进展。在这其中，研究光学体系中的拓扑态催生出了拓扑光子学这一前沿研究领域。 相较于传统光学器件，拓扑光学器件具有对缺陷不敏感和传输鲁棒性等独特优势，未来可应用于光学芯片和拓扑激光等领域。在本次讲座中，主讲人将介绍在磁性光子晶体中的系列进展，包括非成对狄拉克点、反手性拓扑边缘态、无序拓扑光学绝缘体、光学拓扑安德森绝缘体以及三维光学陈绝缘体等。
Measuring the spectral properties of an optical frequency comb is among the most fundamental tasks of precision metrology. In contrast to general single- parameter measurement schemes， we demonstrate here single shot multi-parameter estimation of an optical frequency comb at and beyond the standard quantum limit. The mean energy and the central frequency as well as the spectral bandwidth of ultrafast pulses are simultaneously determined with a multi-pixel spectrally resolved (MPSR) apparatus， without changing the photonics architecture. Moreover， using a quantum frequency comb that intrinsically consists of multiple squeezed states in a family of Hermite- Gaussian spectral/temporal modes， the signal-to-noise ratios of the multiple spectral parameters estimation can surpass the standard quantum limit. Combining our multi-pixel detection scheme and the multimode entangled resource could find applications in ultrafast quantum metrology and multimode quantum information processing.
微腔激子极化激元(exciton-polariton)是一种 半光半物质的准粒子，由光学微腔中的光子与腔内发光材料中的激子通过强耦合作用形成。本报告中，我将简述微腔激子极化激元的基本概念及其自旋光子学(spinoptronics) 相关研究概况，并重点介绍近年来我们在此研究领域的一系列工作，包括圆形势阱中极化激元凝聚的自旋涡旋态与斯格明子态、微腔与偏振各向异性激子材料相结合产生的宏观旋光性，以及在此基础上观测到的非平庸拓扑能谷、极化激元能带上的非厄米奇异点与发散量子度规等有趣现象。微腔自旋光子学对于实现光子芯片上以手性为基础的各类拓扑光子学效应，具有重要的意义。
In analogy to matter， the interaction of ultrashort pulses induces vivid multi-pulse dynamics.As a result， the ultrashort pulses can evolve into various self-assembled pulses such as the soliton molecule， soliton crystal， soliton bunch etc. These pulse complexes can also extend the application scenarios of ultrafast lasers. In this talk， we will first report on our current research progress on the molecular dynamics of self-assembled pulses assisted with the time- stretch and time-lens analysis to answer the question of how far the light-matter analogy could reach. On this basis， flexible manipulation on the self-assembled pulses is also realized， particularly highlighting the phase-tailored assembly of the soliton molecules governed by the subtle energy flows. F or the applied stimuli， advanced soliton encoding beyond binary， ultrafast noise-like-pulse laser ranging and real-time spectral interferometry based sensing applications are also presented.
光纤化学传感技术是以光纤为传导媒介，以光场为感知载体，将待测化学物质信号转换为光信号的变化。光场感知的本质实际上就是光场与物质的相互作用，由此，光纤化学传感技术也面临着两大挑战，一是，受限于作用强度，很难实现化学物质痕量检测，二是，依赖于敏感材料，很难实现化学物质特异性识别。这就带来灵敏度低、可靠度差两大共性难题。近几年报告人为突破光纤化学传感技术中感知灵敏度和识别可靠度两大技术瓶颈，围绕光场时空调控机理和光材协同操控机制两个关键科学问题，分别利用时域慢光、空间光导、光材互耦、光材集成，在机理、技术、方法、工艺上进行创新研究，以实现感知灵敏度提高和识别可靠度增强的目标。本次报告将具体介绍这两方面的代表性成果。
Fiber optic broadband acoustic sensors have great potential applications in many civil and military fields， such as oil and gas pipeline leakage monitoring， high-precision photoacoustic spectrum detection， seismic wave monitoring and anti-submarine monitoring. Compared with the traditional electronic acoustic sensor， optical fiber acoustic sensor has the advantages of high sensitivity， resistant to strong electromagnetic interference， light weight， small size， resistant to corrosion and other irreplaceable advantages. The research of broadband acoustic sensor based on fiber-membrane composite devices structure has been conducted to achieve the goal of high sensitivity， high precision， fast response， ultra-wideband and small size of the acoustic sensor. Four different broadband acoustic sensors based on fiber-membrane composite devices have been designed. It can be divided into two categories: the one broadband acoustic sensor is based on the transmission-type special optical fiber device combined with membrane， and the other ultra-wideband acoustic sensor is based on the reflective EFPI structure combined with the membrane.
Interacting many-electron problems pose some of the greatest computational challenges in science， with essential applications across many fields. The solutions to these problems will offer accurate predictions of chemical reactivity. and kinetics， and other properties of quantum systems. F ermionic quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) methods; which use a statistical sampling of the ground state， are among the most powerful approaches to these problems. Controlling the fermionic sign problem with constraints ensures the efficiency of QMC at the expense of potentially significant biases owing to the limited flexibility of classical computation. We proposed an approach that combined constrained QMC with quantum computation to reduce such biases and we implemented our scheme experimentally using up to 16 qubits to unbias constrained QMC calculations performed on. chemical systems with as many as 120 orbitals. These experiments represent the largest chemistry simulations performed with the help of quantum computers (or at least they did at the time)， while achieving accuracy that is competitive with state- of-the-art classical methods without burdensome error mitigation. Compared with the popular variational quantum eigensolver， our hybrid quantum-classical computational model offers an alternative path towards achieving a practical quantum advantage for the electronic structure problem without demanding exceedingly accurate preparation and measurement of the ground-state wavefunction. In this talk we discuss some of the challenges and prospects for building upon our original result.
Emotions and social interactions color our lives and shape our behaviors.Using animal models and engineered manipulations， we aim to .understand how social and emotional behaviors are encoded in the brain， focusing on the neural circuits underlying dominance hierarchy and depression. This lecture will highlight our recent discoveries on how downward social mobility leads to depression; how ketamine tames depression by blocking burst firing in the brain' s anti-reward center;and， how glia-neuron interaction plays a surprising role in this process. I will also present our recent work on the mechanism underlying the sustained antidepressant activity of ketamine and its brain region specificity. With these results， we hope to illuminate on a more unified theory on ketamine' S mode of action and inspire new treatment strategies for depression.

To construct π molecules with different structures is one of the key points in the research field of opto-electronic materials. In many cases， the molecular structure not only affects the intramolecular π-conjugation， but also the intermolecular π-π stacking， to result in the different functionalities. In this talk，some typical examples will be presented to partially demonstrate the interesting different properties with minor or even ignorable structural difference.

以PD1/L1为代表的免疫拮抗点治疗在多种恶性肿瘤的治疗获得优异的效果，改变治疗模式。但总体有效率低和治疗耐受是临床需要解决的关键问题。双特异抗体可阻断2个靶点，是近年来生物工程技术的前沿方向。TGFb是肿瘤微环境中重要的免疫副调控因子，构建PD-L1/TGFb双功能性抗体，同时阻断两个免疫抑制信号，重塑免疫微环境，通过协同增效，有望扩大PD1/L1的治疗谱，延缓耐药性。
Quantum Ising models have been extensively used to study properties of strongly correlated systems with many-body interactions and to find solutions to NP-hard problems such as combinatorial optimization problems， A controlla ble quantum simulator that faithfully encodes spin Hamiltonians of interest with coherent manipulation and site-resolving detection can address classically intractable problems. Trapped ion systems have reliably demonstrated quantum simulation of various quantum spin models in one-dimensional (1D) chains. Extension of the dimension of the trapped-ion simulator while maintaining the capabilities of 1D chains has been an enticing next step for decades. Here， we present the first quantum simulations of Ising models with two-dimensional (2D) ion crystals in a Paul trap. We benchmark the simulator by implementing various spin models with complex interaction networks and preparing the corresponding ground states adiabatically. In our 2D ion crystal， retaining the advantages of 1D chains， various spin-spin interactions with different signs and sufficiently large strengths are generated by driving different vibrational modes. Quantum coherence of the simulation is probed by reversing the ramping profile of the transverse field to the initial value and then measuring the extent to which the remaining state coincides with the initial state. Then， we benchmark the scalability of the system for the large-scale quantum simulation. We observe major portions of the spin states are in the ground state even for highly frustrated spin models and characterize the corresponding phase with order parameters such as structure factor in 2D. Our results open the door to quantum simulations that can reach far beyond classical computational capability using 2D crystals of ions.
自上世纪八十年代末高温超导材料问世以来，其卓越的微波性能立即受到微波电子工程学界的关注。以YBCO和DBCO为代表的高温超导薄膜微波表面阻抗比铜等良导体低两到三个数量级，这种优势可以延伸至毫米波段。基于高温超导薄膜材料的超导滤波器具有低插损、高选择性、窄相对带宽和高带外抑制的优点，有望替代LTCC滤波器，为超导量子计算的噪声信号抑制提供更为优异的解决方案。此外，在超导量子计算机中，超导滤波器可免去复杂臃肿的制冷、真空和绝热等支撑系统，充分发挥其性能优势。本报告将首先介绍高温超导滤波器的应用背景，然后对滤波器的设计方法及滤波系统的结构进行介绍。最后，将介绍研究团队在宽阻带高抑制超导滤波器方面的成果及应用，着重介绍一款阻带延伸至51倍截止频率的低通滤波器和一款阻带延伸至17倍中心频率的带通滤波器。
This talk introduces a new type of dynamic amplifier， the floating inverter amplifier (FIA). FIA enables current reuse and dynamic biasing， thus achieving excellent energy efficiency. It provides robust operation against process， voltage， and temperature (PVT) variations. Moreover， its output common-mode voltage is well controlled without the need for an explicit common-mode feedback circuit. A few design examples will be discussed: 1) the world's most energy efficient dynamic comparator， 2) the world's first high-performance closed-loop dynamic amplifier，and 3) a pipelined SAR ADC realizing 100x bandwidth adaption.
Since its introduction， soft robotics have enabled many useful features that the conventional rigidones could not achieve before. Among various types， small-scale soft robotics attract attention as they can adaptively enter and explore many highly valuable while confined， hard-to-reach environments.These environments include those inside the human body， ruins of the man-made structure after an earthquake， and many complex natural terrains.In view of such potential， this seminar will first give a bird's view of my research on addressing four key challenges of miniature soft robots. They are (1) Locomotion， (2) Functions， (3) Fabrication， and (4)Materials/Actuators. As an example of the synergistic nature of these investigations， the central part of the presentation will focus on one of my latest research topics: soft miniature robotic devices for future vascular applications. A total of four projects will show three versions of stent-shape robots ' (stentbots) and a robotic guidewire. These robotic devices will demonstrate their potential to safely transverse through the torturous vasculature system and implement various medical functions. With such capability， these devices can be good candidates to supplement our current minimally invasive medical toolbox that can better diagnose， control， and cure various vascular diseases.
Soliton operation of fiber lasers has been a hot research topic. It is well-known that under suitable conditions the soliton operation of a fiber laser could mimic those of the nonlinear Schrodinger equation (NL .SE) soliton dynamics. In particular， when the laser cavity birefringence is considered， the laser dynamics should be described by the coupled NL SEs， which admit various forms of vector soliton solutions， including the group velocity locked vector solitons， phase-locked vector solitons and dark-bright vector solitons. Based on a simple ring cavity erbium-doped fiber laser， we have experimentally demonstrated different forms of the incoherently coupled vector solitons in fiber lasers， these include the group velocity locked bright-bright， dark-dark， and dark-bright solitons. The features of the observed vector solitons could be well described by the incoherently coupled NL SEs. In this talk we further report on the experimental demonstration of different forms of vector solitons formed as a result of the coherent cross-polarization coupling. We have first experimentally confirmed the existence of black-black and black-white vector solitons. The vector solitons formed under coherent cross polarization coupling have distinctly different features from those of the vector solitons formed under the incoherent cross-polarization coupling. They constitute a completely new group of vector solitons formed in fiber lasers.
The phonon coupling in the solid is a fundamental and universal interaction aimong all the material systems. The phonon wave can be. excited by piezoelectric coupling， Raman scattering， or optomechanical interaction which are usually strongly . confined and can easily interact with varied physical systems. I will introduce approaches to engineering the interactions between phonon and photon in the solid-state system， especially the bilayer WSe2: the surface phonon/ acoustic wave can interact with the interlayer exciton. As the result， phonon waves can transport these charge-neutral particles with a long propagation distance of up to 20 microns. Meanwhile， a strong single exciton-phonon interaction has been demonstrated in the strained quantum dot of bilayer WSe2 that the localized exciton can couple to the breathing mode of lattice phonon， with the coupling strength controlled by the electric field. Also， I will extend the phonon engineering to the materials system beyond 2D: as an example， the. spins in the diamond can form the remote interactions facilitated by the cavity phonon inside the optomechanical crystal. In this talk， I will emphasize the strength of phonon engineering which can effectively control the physical properties of solid-state systems.
Salinity temperature and depth are the most important parameters in physical oceanography applications， because of they are the fundamental parameters of the seawater equation of state. In situ monitoring these parameters is of great importance for process control in manufacturingindustries， pr otection of ecosystems ，prevention of global warming， and especially underwater target monitoring and recognition. An all optical fiber CTD sensor used in seawater based on an OMC is demonstrated. And the OMC is fabricated by fusing and tapering two twisted conventional communication fibers based on the improved flame- brushing method. By monitoring the sensing dips， in situ measurement of salinity， temperature and depth (pressure) in seawater can be realized respectively. The all optical fiber CTD sensor demonstrated here show advantages of easy fabrication， compact structure， high sensitivity， low cost， and compatibility with the optical fiber system， which may find applications in multifunction optical sensors in ocean detections and other applications.
The voltage-gated sodium (Nav) channels are responsible for the initiation and propagation of action potentials. Being associated with a variety of disorders， they are targeted by multiple pharmaceutical drugs and natural toxins. Employing the modern methods of cryo- EM， we determined the near atomic resolution structures of Nav channels from American cockroach (designated NavPaS)， and the human Nav1.4， Nav1.2， Nav1.1， Nav1.8 and Nav1.7 with 11 mutations (designated Nav1.7-M11) in complex with distinct auxiliary subunits， animal toxins and small drugs. These structures reveal the folding principle and structural details of the single-chain eukaryotic Nav channels， elucidate the molecular basis for sodium ion permeation， and establish a framework for rational design of subtype-specific blockers for Nav channels. Comparison of these conformationally distinct structures provides important insights into the electromechanical coupling mechanism of Nav channels and offers the 3D template to map hundredes of disease mutations.
We study the conditions that underlie the asymptotic and exponential convergence of saddle flow dynamics of convex-concave functions to a saddle point. First， we propose a certificate rooted in observability for asymptotic convergence of saddle flows. |t generalizes conventional conditions for convergence， e.g.， strict convexity-concavity， and leads to a novel regularization method that is separable and makes minimal requirements on convexity-concavity for asymptotic convergence. Second， we show that saddle flows' global exponential stability is a direct consequence of strong convexity-concavity， which provides a lower-bound estimate of the convergence rate. This insight explains some existing algorithms'convergence properties for equality constrained convex optimization， e.g.， proximal gradient.It is further exploited to design a novel alternative regularized algorithm that achieves exponential convergence at a rate depending only on the strong convexity of the objective. Our results generalize to saddle flow dynamics with projections on the vector field and have immediate applications in inequality constrained convex optimization， in particular， distributed linear programs and constrained reinforcement learning.
The differentiation of preadipocytes into mature adipocytes is accompanied by the formation of a giant， unilocular lipid droplet (LD). Mechanistically. however， LD biagenesis and adipogenesis are two distinct processes. Congenital generalized lipodystrophy， also known as Berardinelli-Seip congenital lipodystrophy (BSCL)， is characterized by a near complete loss of adipose tissue， severe insulin resistance and hepatic steatosis. BSCL1 encodes a metabolic enzyme， 1-acylglycerol-3-phosphate Oacyltransferase 2/AGPAT2， and BSCL2 encodes seipin， a protein of unknown molecular function. We demonstrate that both AGPAT2 and seipin are required for the normal biogenesis of LDs， in addition to their essential role in adipogenesis. Mechanistically， both AGPAT2 and seipin function to maintain the normal level/distribution of phosphatidic acid in the endoplasmic reticulum (ER) and the inner nuclear membrane: seipin inhibits the activity of ER-localized glycerol-3-phosphate O-acyltransferases 3/4 (GPAT3/4) whereas AGPAT2 promotes the stability and activity of CDP-diacylglycerol synthases. Our results suggest that the level and distribution of phospholipids， e.g. phosphatidic acid， play important roles in both LD biogenesis and adipogenesis.
Quantum transduction is an essential ingredient in scaling up distributed quantum architecture and is actively pursued based on various physical platforms. In this talk， I will first briefly introduce the concept of quantum transduction. Then I will discuss our recent approach for transduction， which relaxes the im pedance matching condition to half impedance matching condition， and it can be achieved by introducing a two-photon drive in given transducers. We show the transduction channel capacity is enhanced and can be understood in a simple interference picture with the help of Bloch-Messiah decomposition. The parameter regimes with positive quantum capacity are identified and compared with and without the drive， indicating that the parametric drive-induced enhancement is promising in demonstrating quantum state conversion， and is expected to boost the performance of transduction with various physical platforms.
紧密结合国际前沿和国家重大需求，聚焦项目的科学意义，凝练核心科学问题。针对核心科学问题，详细阐述国内外发展动态。根据关键科学问题的国内外发展动态，提出研究目标、梳理研究内容。围绕研究内容，遴选研究方法、设计技术路线。通过研究基础、科研能力技术储备，论证方案的可行性。总结项目的创新和特色，明确成果的原创性.
1.The interaction of proteins with metabolites and other proteins underlies most if not all cellular activities， and many bioactive xenobiotics perturb cellular processes through direct physical interactions with proteins.Mapping these biomolecular interactions can help unravel the complex protein machines and molecular pathways underlying various cellular processes， to systematically unveil wiring of the cells that are dysregulated in diseases and perturbed by chemicals.Nevertheless， there are currently limited time- and cost-effective techniques for profiling intracellular protein-protein and protein-chemical interactions at scale and in situ. My laboratory integrates methods in computational sciences， analytical chemistry and molecular biology with new protein cellular biophysics techniques for large-scale profiling of protein-protein and protein-chemical interactions. Tedious chemical derivatization and genetic engineering are avoided which facilitate rapid deployment of our methods for systematic investigation of various biological phenomena including deciphering the mechanism-of-action of bioactive chemicals andtherapeutic agents. I will describe these methods developed in my laboratory， as well as our recent findings deploying them for proteome-wide screens for off-targets and perturbed protein-protein interactions for hundreds of bioactive compounds and FDA approved drugs.2.Researchers commonly anneal metals， alloys， and semiconductors to repair defects and im prove microstructures via recrystallization. Theoretical studies indicate simulated annealing on biological macromolecules helps predict the final structures with minimum free energy. Experimental validation of this homogenizing effect and further exploration of its applications are fascinating scientific questions that remain elusive. Here， we chose the apo-state 70S ribosome from Escherichia coli as a model， wherein the 30S subunit undergoes a thermally driven inter-subunit rotation and exhibits substantial structural flexibility as well as distinct free energy. We experimentally demonstrate that annealing at a fast cooling rate enhances the 70S ribosome homogeneity and improves local resolution on the 30S subunit. After annealing， the 70S ribosome is in a nonrotated state with respect to corresponding intermediate structures in unannealed or heated ribosomes， and exhibits a minimum energy in the free energy landscape. Our experimental results are consistent with theoretical analysis on the temperature-dependent Boltzmann distribution， and offer a facile yet robust approach to enhance protein stability， which is ideal for high-resolution cryogenic electron microscopy.
We will first introduce a method which spatially profiled epigenomes in single cells and provided high-throughput and high-resolution measurements of spatial distributions of active promoters and putative enhancers in embryonic and adult mouse brains. Our results further revealed putative enhancer hubs regulating the expression of developmentally important genes. We will also describe an imaging-based pooled CRISPR screening approach that combines high-content phenotype imaging with single guide RNA (sgRNA) identification in individual cells. We used this approach to screen RNA-binding proteins for their effects on RNA localization to nuclear compartments and revealed both positive and negative regulators for the nuclear speckle localization of a long noncoding RNA， MALAT1， suggesting a dynamic regulation of IncRNA localization in subcellular compartments.
RNA plays a pivotal role in gene expression， understanding RNA'S functionality is of fundamentalimportance for molecular biology. Revealing RNA structure provides a powerful way to gain mechanical insights of RNA's function in gene regulation. By aligning chemical profiling and high-throughput sequencing， we have developed powerful methods to determine both canonical and noncanonical RNA structures in living plants. Our studies have revealed pervasive functions of RNA structure in regulation alternative splicing， translation and environmental sensing in plants. 植原体是一类由刺吸式口器昆虫传播的植物韧皮部专性细菌性病害，可以侵染上千种植物，包括大多数粮食作物，蔬菜，林木以及果树。有意思的是，植原体常常会引起植物宿主发育上的剧烈变化，包括让植物的花变成叶子( phylloly)或者让植物产生小叶和丛枝(Witches' broom)等症状，使得植物无法正常生长繁殖，最终沦为植原体滋生和传播的温床，又被称为‘僵尸’植物(‘Zombie'plant)。本报告将围绕植原体效应蛋白的功能研究，阐述效应蛋白如何通过非泛素化依赖的蛋白酶体降解途径调控植物发育，从而促进病原菌在自然界中传播。
In the era of 4th industrial revolution， the importance of internet of things (IoT)， which is the network of physical objects， has been rapidly growing. Among many core components for loT， sensors measure physical parameters and status of objects including pressure， strain， temperature， pH， gas concentration， etc. As more sensors are deployed in numerous objects， especially in remote places， the power supply for the sensor operation is becoming a highly challenging issue. Accordingly， a.number. of low-power or self-powered sensors are being actively developed. In this talk， I will introduce recent development of self-powered physical and chemical sensors at our research group.
Surface plasmon resonance sensors are commonly used an effective tool for real-time monitoring biomolecular interactions. The sensing mechanism is based on the evanescent field perturbation at the metallic sensing substrate induced by the binding of chemical and biological molecules. Molecular binding interactions could be measured from the signal of reflected light， under the condition that the surface plasmon resonance is excited by the incident light. In this talk， I will present the use of hybrid 2D nanomaterials-based metasurface nanostructure as an enhanced sensing substrate. The thickness of the plasmonic sensing substrate is tuned in an atomic scale and optimized to improve the sensing capability. Here， both a sharp phase signal change and phase-related Goos-Hanchen signal shift were achieved due to the strong resonance at the surface of the sensing film. The enhanced plasmonic sensitivities of 2D nanostructures were systematically investigated. It is worth noting that the tunability of atomic layer led to the sensing substrate optimized with a narrow scale < 1 nm. Through a precise engineering of the metasurface substrates， 3 orders of magnitude improvement of the sensitivity were demonstrated compared to the one with pure gold sensing substrate. This hybrid 2D nanomaterial-based metasurfaces would provide a good opportunity for developing portable theranostic devices in clinical applications.

创新创业大讲堂邀请原中石化集团董事长、原中国海洋石油有限公司董事长、碳中和国际研究院创始人、长江商学院CEO联盟主席傅成玉，作题为《碳中和——中国现代化建设新内涵》的报告。
量子多体物理体系在远离平衡态时会涌现出意想不到的集体行为。我们在实验上首次发现当原子间的相互作用被周期性的调制时，原子喷射流从二维的玻色爱因斯坦凝聚体(BEC)中产生，形如烟花。类似于激光产生的原理，"玻色烟花”源于物质波在BEC作为增益介质下的受激辐射。即使局域的原子计数显示的是热分布，整个体系却处在一个二模压缩态:处在相反动量模式的原子具有长程的关联和纠缠。通过在相互作用调制中加入两种相称的频率，我们成功制备出六模压缩态并通过原子喷流与BEC干涉形成的密度波来验证这六个动量模式在幅度和相位上的关联性。另外，我们演示了这种相互作用调制的技术能够被用来测量非均匀和旋转的BEC量子态。另一方面我们通过调节原子间的碰撞共振点一Feshbach共振一首次实现了原子BEC到带有轨道角动量的二维分子BEC的相变。在合成分子的淬火动力学过程中，我们观测到分子的相干振荡并且其振荡频率随着原子BEC密度的增加而变快这是化学反应中玻色增强效应的证据。最后，我将介绍一个全新而强大的体系一多 模腔量子电动力学-其中腔内的多模光场介导的调控性极高的原子间相互作用可以提供研究自旋玻璃等量子物态及解决组合优化问题和研究神经网络中的联想记忆的理想平台。
大量临床研究表明，夜间睡眠静息心率、呼吸、心率变异的精准、连续、长期监测，对心血管及睡眠呼吸类疾病的早发现及预后评估具有重要意义。相较穿戴式设备，非接触心率、呼吸监测因用户主观舒适性高得到普遍关注。本次报告将介绍基于压力传感的非接触式睡眠心率、呼吸监测技术及其在慢病筛查中的应用。
肺动脉高压(Pulmonaryhypertension，PH)是-组以肺动脉压力及肺血管阻力进行性升高为主要特征的综合征，最终导致患者右心衰竭甚至死亡。压电式机械敏感离子通道组件1 ( Piezo Type Mechanosensitive lon Channel Component， Piezo1)是一种与血管重塑有关的重要机械敏感通道，它可以通过各种形式的机械刺激(例如流动剪切、膜拉伸)来激活。王健课题组通过左肺动脉结扎(LPAL)建立肺动脉高压大鼠的2周和5周模型，以模拟高流量和血流动力学应激诱导下的肺动脉高压。与假手术对照组(SHAM)大鼠相比，LPAL大鼠全肺组织中Piezo1的表达上调，且在LPAL -2w和LPAL-5w大鼠的肺动脉平滑肌细胞(PASMCs)中观察到Piezo1的上调与胞质Ca2+浓度([Ca2+]cyt)的增加有关。通过机制探究发现: LPAL大鼠PASMCs中Piezo1的上调与Yes相关蛋白(YAP)/TEA结构域转录因子4 (TEAD4)直接相关;而Piezo1 的肺动脉内皮细胞(PAECs)上调与RELA (p65)的转录调节和肺部炎症有关。该研究揭示了Piezo1在调控PASMCs和ECs中的联合作用，通过不同的细胞信号通路协调，导致LPAL-肺动脉高压大鼠肺血管重塑，为Piezo1在剪切应力相关实验性肺动脉高压中的细胞类型特异性致病作用提供了新的见解。
肺动脉高压由各种病因引起肺血管收缩和重塑、肺血管阻力和压力进行性升高，以致右心衰竭甚至死亡的一种严重危害人类健康的重大慢性疾病。围绕细胞外钙感受器(calcium-sensing receptor， CaSR)，一种G蛋白耦联受体，在肺血管收缩和重塑中机制作用所开展的系列性研究发现，缺氧通过线粒体源性活性氧增强CaSR敏感性，介导缺氧肺血管收缩和肺动脉压力升高(2012) ;移植体血管线粒体可抑制缺氧肺血管收缩、重塑和肺动脉高压(2016a; 2016b; 2022) ; hypoxia-induced mitogenic factor与CaSR胞内段结合持续活化CaSR，诱导肺动脉高压，运用人工穿膜多肽阻断二者的结合可选择性缓解缺氧诱导的肺动脉高压(2017) ;野百合碱激活肺动脉内皮细胞CaSR、引起内皮损伤、触发肺动脉高压(2017) ;野百合碱与静脉血红细胞结合、随血流转运至肺血管，在肺毛细血管前动脉从红细胞上脱落，随即结合、激活内皮细胞膜CaSR (2019) ;吸烟诱导肺动脉内皮细胞携带精胺的细胞外囊泡释放，结合、激活肺动脉平滑肌细胞CaSR，引起肺动脉高压(2019);利用人工多肽阻断急性缺氧诱导的CaSR自聚合可缓解缺氧肺动脉高压(2021) ;食物源性香叶基香叶基焦磷酸通过拮抗他汀抑制的CaSR相关信号通路，抵消他汀对肺动脉高压的治疗作用(2021);CaSR遗传变异增加肺动脉高压患者易感性(2022)。
基于原子分子系综的精密测量在基础物理和实际应用中发挥着很重要的作用。原子磁强计具有较高的灵敏度，对超高精度磁场测量具有重要意义，广泛应用于生物医学、古地磁探索、航空磁探测、宇宙轴子自旋进动实验、探测类磁场效应等领域;核磁共振陀螺仪是用来探测角速度的传感器，由: 于其高精度、 小体积等优势，有望成为战术级、导航级载体的陀螺仪，是未来高精度、微小型陀螺仪的重要研究对象。同位素Th-229是已知唯一在几个电子伏特的能量范围内具有激发态的原子核，这种独特的条件使得现有激光技术激发核跃迁成为可能。基于Th-229核跃迁的核钟对外界电磁场的干扰较小，精度有望超越现在所有的原子钟，将成为探测精细结构常数a随着时间变化最灵敏的传感器。
Phonons are carriers of both information and energy. They are main heat carriers in semiconductors and dielectric materials. In this talk， Prof. Li will answer the following questions: (1) why thermal conductivity in low dimensional materials diverges with system size? (2) What is connection between divergent (anomalous) thermal conductivity and anomalous diffusion? (3) How reliable are experimental techniques in measuring thermal conductivity in nano scale? We consider to model matrix time series based on a tensor CP-decomposition. ! Instead of using an iterative algorithm which is the standard practice for estimating CP-decompositions， we propose a new and one-pass estimation procedure based on a generalized eigenanalysis constructed from the serial dependence structure of the underlying process. To overcome the intricacy of solving a rank-reduced generalized eigenequation， we propose a further refined approach which projects it into a lower-dimensional full-ranked eigenequation. This refined method improves significantly the finite-sample performance of the estimation. The asymptotic theory has been established under a general setting without the stationarity. It shows， for example， that all the component coefficient vectors in the CP-decomposition are estimated consistently with certain convergence rates. The proposed model and the estimation method are also illustrated with both simulated and real data; showing effective dimension-reduction in modelling and forecasting matrix time series.
In this study， we examine whether managers learn from share prices when conducting corporate R&D. We exploit the context of China which has been undergoing a transition from“Made in China”to“Innovated in China”， and has seen substantial growth in national wide R&D intensity since 2012. By constructing a sector-year level R&D premium- the valuation difference between high-R&D and low-R&D firms， we find a significantly positive association between the R&D premium and subsequent corporate R&D expenditures within the sector. The premium-driven corporate R&D becomes more pronounced when managers have greater incentives to glean information from share prices， i.e.， for (1) firms with higher managerial equity ownership， (2)firms more dependent on equity financing and (3) non-state-owned firms. Using China 's initiation of the STAR board in 2018， which facilitates listing for innovative firms in selected industries， as an exogenous shock to R&D premiums， we perform difference- in-differences analyses and obtain empirical evidence that favors a causal claim. Finally， we find that the outcomes of corporate R&D， i.e.， more patent applications， patents granted and higher firm growth， do not deteriorate with R&D premiums， supporting rational managerial learning rather than opportunistic catering.
This paper examines how options traders trade daily stock market mispricing measured by short-term past return and put-call option volatility spread. Anomaly return is 7.31 basis points per day when customer option traders trade along with the anomaly signal and is insignificant when they trade against it. This effect is more pronounced for out-of-money options. We show that the delta-hedging activities by option market makers and copycat trades by other institutional investors associated with customer options trades help the correction of mispricing.
Change is the only constant in reality. Detecting changes and making statistical inferences based onlocal stationarity is vital in a stochastic data sequence. As in analyzing network and shape data， the events that change are not always characterized as objects in a Euclidean space. There is a growing importance and urgency to analyze the dynamics in the time series of data objects in a non- Euclidean space. However， existing methods are predominantly developed for Euclidean data by using the characteristics of Euclidean spaces. There is little research on whether existing methods are useful for non-Euclidean sequences. Through simulation studies of manifold-valued sequences and dynamic network sequences， we demonstrate that existing methods do not perform well in detecting dynamical changes of probability measures(regimes) in non- Euclidean sequences. Thus， it is imperative to develop methods to detect dynamical regime changes in non- Euclidean sequences effectively.To this end， we introduce a nonparametric and hierarchical approach that identifies time points at which an abrupt change occurs in the probability measure of non-Euclidean data in metric spaces. Our approach is also practical for Euclidean data.Using the metric， we define a metric based binary partition function that reaches the maximum at a change point. We not only show that our approach can estimate the number of change-points and detect their locations consistently but also provide that the convergence rate of the estimated change points is OP (1/T)， which is optimal. Extensive simulation studies and analysis of a real dataset demonstrate that our method has considerable advantages over state-of-the-art methods， especially when data are non- Euclidean or covariance structures change over time.
随着移动互联网和传感技术的发展，我们每个人每天都在不断产生丰富的数据。这些数据可以定量地记录我们生活的多个方面，消费，饮食，运动和健康，等等，并通过可视化的形式转化成信息，反馈给用户自己。在越来越多以数据为中心的智能产品中，目前的可视化设计多数重视信息的有效表达，而用户在获得和使用数据过程中的体验并没有得到足够的重视。因此， 数据体验设计，作为一个新的设计领域，正在尝试将数据作为设计物料，以用户为中心，基于不同使用情境和数据内容，通过可视化和人机交互设计的创新，增强数据可视化的美学和意义，以及创造新的用户体验。 于滨博士将通过众多设计案例来分析他在数据体验设计中的经验和体会。

Before each IC digital design tape out， we will need to run various checks to make sure the design have sufficient margins for timings， noises and supplies.The margins are needed since desgin is mostly based on fixed conditions or parameters. In reality， even on the same die， there will be significant on-chip variations or uncertainties of the parameters. In this topic， I will introduce the basic methods to derive and define these sign-off margins.
DNA甲基化是一类稳定遗传的表观修饰，在动植物基因组中广泛存在。不同组织和细胞内的DNA甲基化模式对基因调控、转座沉默及基因印记十分重要。不同位点、组织或细胞内的DNA甲基化模式的调控机制，是表观遗传学的基本问题。拟南芥中染色质重塑因子CLASSY家族四个成员对DNA甲基化模式的建立至关重要。研究表明，这四个CLSY基因在拟南芥中呈现明显的组织表达特异性，它们是调控拟南芥组织特异性DNA甲基化模式的主要因子。CLSYs对植物不同位点和组织间DNA甲基化模式的调控，为利用表观遗传机制改良作物提供了可能性。
在高等植物配子发育的过程中，染色质高级结构发生了深刻的变化。花粉，是植物的雄配子体，含有精子细胞和营养核，负责将精子运送至雌性生殖器官，以完成受精，繁衍后代。精子细胞和营养核是由共同的前体细胞仅仅经过1或2次有丝分裂发育而来，然而，它们的染色质结构却差别巨大。营养核的染色质高度疏松，而精子的染色质高度浓缩，其分子机制并不清楚。我们的研究显示两种组蛋白变异体(组蛋白H1和H2B.8)均通过相分离的机制分别浓缩异染色质和常染色质，并参与花粉染色质高级结构的重塑，这对植物的生殖至关重要。
Autonomous driving has shown great potential to reform modern transportation. Yet its reliability and safety have drawn a lot of attention and concerns. Compared with traditional software systems， autonomous driving systems (ADSs) often use deep neural networks in tandem with logic-based modules. This new paradigm poses unique challenges for software testing. Despite the recent development of new ADS testing techniques， it is not clear to what extent those techniques have addressed the needs of ADS practitioners. To fill this gap， we have published a few works and I will present some of them. The first work is to reduce and prioritize test for multi-module autonomous driving systems (Accepted in FSE'22， CCF A). The second work is to conduct comprehensive study to identify the current practices， needs and gaps in testing autonomous driving systems (Accepted also in FSE'22， CCF A). The third work is to analyze the robustness issues in the deep learning driving models (Accepted in PerCom'20， CORE A*). The fourth work is to generate test cases from traffic rules for autonomous driving models (Accepted in TSE 22， CCF A). I will also cover some ongoing and future work in autonomous driving systems.
Recent experiments have demonstrated that rapid rupture fronts， akin to earthquakes， mediate the transition to frictional motion.Moreover， once these dynamic rupture fronts ("laboratory earthquakes") are created， their singular form， dynamics and arrest are well-described by fracture mechanics. Ruptures， however， need to be created within initially rough frictional interfaces， before they are able to propagate. This is the reason that "static friction coefficients" are not well-defined; frictional ruptures can nucleate for a wide range of applied forces. A critical open question is， therefore， how the nucleation of rupture fronts actually takes place. We experimentally demonstrate that rupture front nucleation is prefaced by slow nucleation fronts. These nucleation fronts， which are self-similar， are not described by our current understanding of fracture mechanics. The nucleation fronts emerge from initially rough frictional interfaces at well-defined stress thresholds， evolve at characteristic velocity and time scales governed by stress levels， and propagate within a frictional interface to form the initial rupture from which fracture mechanics take over. These results are of fundamental importance to questions ranging from earthquake nucleation and prediction to processes governing material failure.

自上世纪中叶以来，计算机和计算芯片以晶体管为基本元件构建数字处理电路，摩尔定律驱动计算性能增长。而当晶体管尺寸微缩接近物理极限，摩尔定律面临终结，芯片算力增长逐渐放缓，人类正在步入后摩尔时代。此外，以CPU、GPU为代表的传统芯片架构下计算单元与存储单元的分离也造成频繁的数据搬运，形成速度、功耗瓶颈(冯诺依曼瓶颈)， 在近年来兴起的神经网络等数据密集型计算任务上问题进一步凸显。 未来智能计算需求仍面临指数增长，传统计算架构瓶颈更加突出， 亟需从器件创新、架构创新层面为后摩尔时代算力持续增长提供新的驱动力。近年来，通过存算一体、 类脑计算等新型计算范式构建具有高效智能计算芯片与系统已经取得了显著进展。然而在现有计算系统下全部智能、复杂性、适应性都是由软件编程(事实上是编程的生物智能体-人)所赋予的，器件、电路本身均不具备任何复杂性与适应性。与之相比，生物系统展示出了分子、细胞、系统等多层次、全方位的智能、复杂性与适应性，对于发展新一代智能、高效计算技术具有重要启发意义。

1.离子在智能生命体中至关重要，神经细胞中动作电位的产生、植物细胞光合作用、皮肤的压力感知等都和离子的定向传输密切相关。可以说，智能生命的语言是“离子”，而人工智能的语言是“电子”。因此，如何构筑基于离子传输的能源与传感体系，从而架起智能生命和仿生体系的桥梁，是我们未来面向人工智能的一个重要挑战。该研究方向是受生物蛋白质通道及其离子输运功能的启发，近年来随着纳米科学与技术的发展而兴起的最前沿和最活跃的课题之一。围绕可控离子传输及其功能应用这一目标，我们通过仿生的手段构筑了一系列离子传输材料，通过调控其结构和界面性质，探究了限域纳米空间内可控离子传输的机制，构筑了基于离子传输的能源和传感器件。在此基础上，我们进一步在多尺度范围内实现了基于离子传输的可穿戴器件、仿生神经元、脑机接口电极等神经拟态器件，最终希望实现“人工智能-生物智能”无障碍沟通的目标。2. 目前市场与临床上对可穿戴器件与植入式器件的需求日益剧增，如何使器件具有良好的生物相容性，组织适应性以及稳定耐用性成为了亟待解决的问题。我们在这里研究了一种金属-聚合物导体的新材料，在运动采集、电化学分析、电生理信号监测以及基因质粒递送等方面进行了创新和优化。由于其优秀的柔性与拉伸性，良好的生物相容性以及简单高效的制备方法，该柔性电子在生物医学领域具有非常广阔的应用前景。本报告将介绍近年来我们在柔性电子-生物医学领域的成果和探索。
文化产业已成为提升城市综合竞争力的新引擎，如何评估城市文化产业发展状况，对城市管理者而言非常关键。在深圳市宣传文化事业发展专项基金的持续资助下，创立于2012年 的中国城市创意指数(Chinese City Creativity Index， CCCI)已由深圳大学周志民团队连续11年定期进行研究与发布。基于波特的钻石模型、系统论、Interbrand晶 牌评估法等相关理论方法，周志民团队构建了一个由要素推动力、需求拉动力、发展支撑力和产业影响力等4大模块、11个二级指标和28个三级指标构成的中国城市创意指数模型。该模型在考虑了人才、经费、科技、文化等资源推动的同时，还考虑了文化需求和消费潜力的拉动作用，以及通讯、网络等相关行业的支撑作用，整体评估城市在文化创意方面的影响力。CCCI是国内首个跨城市对比的文化产业竞争力指数，也是我国跨地域文化产业对比研究领域的重要成果。12月4日，中国城市创意指数第1 1次发布。在本次讲座中，主讲人周志民教授将讲述他是如何构建中国城市创意指数(CCCI) 模型以及如何对其进行测量。

先进制造是重要工业基础，是实体经济的核心支撑点，其中关键数学理论与方法相关研究已经列入十四五规划，同时也给出多个项目支持。它涉及的研究领域十分广泛，其中几何数字化设计与分析是核心问题之一，包含计算几何，几何设计与分析，图形图像数据处理，路径规划与运动控制，几何机器学习等，其中一个共性关键流程就是数理模型建立、分析与求解。这里将简要给出CAD-CAM-CNC数字化智能加工流程中一些问题，供进一步探讨。
病原微生物和宿主植物在长期“博弈”的过程中协同进化。植物具有双层先天免疫系统(innate immune system)来识别病原微生物的入侵，而病原物利用毒性蛋白等致病武器促进侵染。革兰氏阴性细菌通过特化的11型分泌系统，向植物细胞内转运效应子蛋白(effector) ，是一类重要的致病武器。之前大量研究表明很多效应子通过干扰植物的免疫通路而促进侵染。而病原细菌丁香假单胞杆菌( Pseudomonas syringae) 利用一类高度保守的效应子AvrFE， HopM1在植物叶片中诱导水分大量积累而促进侵染。我们近期的工作发现，效应子AvrE靶向拟南芥的I型蛋白磷酸酶家族，从而在侵染的叶片中引起植物脱落酸(abscisic acid) 通路的激活和气孔关闭，从而在叶片细胞间隙诱导“液态水环境”。因此，病原物的一类进化保守的致病因子通过靶向植物脱落酸通路和气孔运动，来改变植物组织生理状态和诱发病害。
植物能够整合精细调控的模式触发式免疫(PTI) 和效应子触发式免疫(ETI) 感知和抵御病原菌。在PTI中， 植物通过细胞膜上的模式识别受体识别病原菌的标志性分子模式(MAMP，例如真菌几丁质和细菌鞭毛)或植物自身产生的损伤分子模式(DAMP，例如植物细胞因子)，进而通过类受体胞质激酶(RLCK) 介导下游信号转导和病原菌抗性。本次报告将介绍植物几丁质受体与RLCK介导几丁质信号转导的分子机制以及几丁质信号通路与鞭毛、细胞因子通路之间的协同调控。

The theory of Mixed-Spin-P fields was introduced by Chang-Li-Li-Liu for the quintic threefold. Chang-Guo-Li has successfully applied it to prove important conjectures on the higher-genus Gromov-Witten invariants. In this talk I will explain a generalization of the construction to more spaces. The key is the stability condition which guarantees the separatedness and properness of certain moduli spaces. It also generalizes the construction of the mathematical Gauged Linear Sigma Model by Fan-Jarvis-Ruan， removing their technical assumption about "good liftings".This is a joint work with Huai-Liang Chang， Shuai Guo， Jun Li and Wei-Ping Li.
Gromov Witten invariants Fg encodes the numbers of genus g curves in Calabi Yau threefolds and play an important role in enumerative geometry. In 1993， Bershadsky， Cecotti， Ooguri， Vafa exhibited a hidden "Feynman structure" governing all Fg’s at once， using path integral methods. The counterpart in mathematics has been missing for many years. After a decades of search， in 2018， a mathematical approach: Mixed Spin P field (MSP) moduli， is finally developed to provide the wanted “Feynman structure”， for quintic CY 3-fold. Instead of enumerating curves in the quintic 3-fold， MSP enumerate curves in a large N dimensional singular space with quintic-3-fold boundary. The “P fields” and “cosections” are used to formulate counting in the singular space via a Landau Ginzburg type construction.In this talk， I shall focus on geometric ideas behind the MSP moduli. Some update will be provided. The results follow from a decade of joint works with Jun Li， Shuai Guo， Young Hoon Kiem， Weiping Li， Melissa C.C. Liu， Jie Zhou， and Yang Zhou.
Expensive problem refers to optimization problems wherein each solution evaluation introduces significant cost， either in the form of computation time or financial investment. Such problems are common in engineering design field due to the use of numerical simulations and physical experiments for design evaluation. Evidently， reducing the number of candidate solution evaluation is of practical interest when developing algorithms to solve such problems.Surrogate modelling and knowledge transfer are among the potential techniques that can be integrated into generic optimization methods for the purpose of controlling the number of solution evaluations. In this talk， I will introduce our recent investigations using these techniques to improve algorithm performance on two classes of problems: multiple-objective problems (MOP) and bilevel optimization problem (BOP). For MOP， the research .observes behaviours of common normalization approaches for an hypervolume-driven surrogate assisted algorithm. From observation， an enhanced normalization process is proposed and improvement on performance is demonstrated across a diverse set of problems. For BOP， the presented study investigates exploiting uncertainty information of surrogate model for infill strategy and its impact on algorithm performance. In addition，relations between neighbour solutions are investigated with the concept of knowledge transfer. Knowledge transfer schemes are proposed to expedite search and their performances are analysed against benchmark problems.
词体兴起而来，雅俗之辨即成为词学批评之一大范畴。由于词与大众娱乐有密切关系，故出现了切合大众口味的俚词，如敦煌曲子词、柳永词、宋代的民间词等，形成了一种独特的美学体系。另一方面，文人则透过对俚词的批评和词集的筛选，力图提高词的审美标准和文学地位。本讲尝试从流行美学及普罗大众的审美角度来解读唐宋俚词，对俚词与雅词作出美学上的区別，并探讨词评家诠释作品的手法，同时分析俚词的艺术风格、形式和內容等方面的特色。
学科交叉研究是当今科学研究与设计创新的发展方向，在自然人机交互、工业设计、信息艺术设计等领域都有着广泛的理论意义和重要的应用价值。随着交叉学科领域研究与创新的飞速发展，设计思维、计算思维、工程思维不断得到深度融合。本次报告将结合清华大学未来实验室在多学科融合与交叉的一些研究进展介绍相关工作。
Prof. Feliks Przytycki will discuss Hausdorff (fractal) dimension of limit Julia sets arising when iterating complex polynomials or rational functions on the Riemann sphere. Methods used， belong to the thermodynamic formalism involving Kolmogorov entropy， Lyapunov exponents and geometric pressure and equilibria. A relation with the boundary behavior of conformal maps on the unit disc will be mentioned.
在以大数据为基础的现代信息社会，硅基光电子已经成为最具潜力的高效率低成本片上解决方案，其应用也从最初的微电子扩展到通信、计算、传感、人工智能、消费、乃至所有的信息系统。信息系统的小型化是信息社会永恒的主题。本报告从信息技术的基本要素出发，详述微电子、光电子的发展历程，论证硅基光电子的必然性，及其对信息系统小型化的关键使能作用。
Climatc-rclated regulations have become increasingly prevalent in countries worldwide.however， due to the global public good nature of climate， it is unclear to what extent these regulations are enforced by individual countries and whether they influence key corporate decisions. We shed light on this issue by examing the impact of climate laws on the international market for corporate control. We find that foreign acquirers are significantly less likely to pursue targets in countries that have enacted climate laws. This effect is : stronger when targets operate in industries more exposed to climate regulations and in countries with stricter legal enforcement， but is weaker for acquirers from countries that are more concerned about climate change or experienced climate disasters. Consistent with a selective enforcement mechanism， the political affinity between the acquirer and target countries attenuates the impact of climate regulations. Furthermore， cross-border deals feature smaller synergies， lower premiums， and less post-merger operating performance improvement after target countries pass climate laws. Deals announced shortly before the enactment of climate laws are more likely to be withdrawn.
Abstract: Industrial Cyber Physical Systems (iCPSs) connect the industrial physical systems (physical world) and the information systems (cyber world) through technologies such as IoT， ICT and big data analysis， to realize real-time perception， dynamic control and information services for large-scale industrial systems. While iCPS brings large scale automation and efficiency to industrial production control， it exposes the industrial control system to the Internet through which cyber attacks can directly affect the normal operations of iCPSs， cause damages to the system infrastructures and even threaten the national security. Therefore， intrusion detection technology needs to be integrated into iCPSs to detect， identify and stop the attacks and minimize the damage to the systems. That is， when attacks are detected， it is necessary to locate the source of the attack， so that further actions can be taken to mitigate the damage of the attacks. This talk will present our investigations into this challenging problem， intrusion detection and localization， through formulating it in a multi-variant time series anomaly detection framework and solving it by using computational intelligence techniques.
Abstract: Edge and cloud resources in virtualized environments are increasingly adopted for enhancing the performance of unmanned cyber-physical systems such as mobile robots and other systems. When multiple robots are deployed in a large geographical area， edge resources in the proximity of robots are used to handle multiple real-time tasks from the robots， thus avoiding large delay from communicating with a cloud center. However， edge resources are energy- and resource-constrained. Therefore， sharing edge resource among multiple real-time robotic tasks with deadline requirements is critical. It is， however， challenging because of the resource and deadline constraints on not only the edge but also the robots. This talk will present our investigations into this challenging problem through formulating it in an optimization framework and solving it by using computational intelligence techniques.
与植物共生的微生物组被认为是植物的第二套基因组，它在植物的生长发育和对环境的适应性等方面发挥着关键的作用。虽然植物微生物组在生产上有巨大的应用潜力，但对植物与微生物组互作机制的研究尚处于起步阶段。我们将围绕高粱根系微生物组展开讨论，探索作物与根系微生物的互作机制以及微生物组在干早下的促生能力。
Plants are colonized by commensal， beneficial， and pathogenic microbes such as bacteria that significantly affect plant health in nature and agricultural fields. Plants require bacterial colonization for their survival in nature， but ironically， some bacteria cause severe disease in plants， pointing to the dilemma that plants face. Therefore， the fundamental question is how plants engage with beneficial bacteria while at the same time restricting pathogenic bacteria. However， despite extensive studies into the molecular and genetic bases of plant immunity， we still lack fundamental knowledge of how plants actually regulate bacterial growth and behavior in plants. We utilized multi-omics and molecular genetics to dissect critical components in both plants and bacteria and underpinned the molecular basis of bacterial regulation by plant immunity. In this seminar， I will discuss some of the recent results and introduce our effort to improve agricultural traits.
王文杰，深圳市投资控股有限公司党委副书记、董事、总经理。毕业于南京大学，高级经济师。曾任职于广州市计划委员会投资处、深圳市投资管理公司投资发展部，先后担任深圳市燃气集团人力资源部部长、副总经理、董事兼总经理等职务，2018年5月起任现职。具有丰富的业务拓展能力、国资国企改革创新经历和企业管理实践经验，个人曾获“2021中国企业改革发展优秀成果特等奖”。
Oceans and seas cover 72% of the earth’ s surface， and they are increasingly being recognized as the next research frontier for sustainable resource management and economic development. The United Nations declared 2021 to 2030 as the“Decade of Ocean Science for Sustainable Development"。The "blue economy”is an emerging concept that envisions the sustainable development of ocean resources while improving societal well-being and equity (World Bank 2017). Central to this is the availability of vast but untapped marine renewable energy for powering the blue economy， including ocean waves， tidal and ocean currents， offshore wind， etc. The power density of wave energy is 10 times as the solar. Intensive research on marine energy has been done since the energy crises in the 1970s and 2000s， however， its widespread adoption is still in infancy because of convergence challenges in engineering， economic， and socio-environmental perspectives. I will mainly present my career path towards ocean energy and the blue economy， including my training and early work on vehicle dynamics and vibration control， industry working on instrumentation， my research on large-scale energy harvesting from civill structures， vehicles， and transportation systems， my recent focus on marine energy involving power takeoff design， hydrodynamics， power electronics， controlco design， wave tank and ocean tests. Iwill also discuss powering the blue economy applications and ongoing work on offshore wind energy. Finally， I will conclude the talk with my vision of driving the research convergence of marine energy through multidisciplinary research collaboration， crosscutting academia-industry-community partnership and multi-dimensional workforce training.
Cellular V2X (C-V2X) communications in 5G enable more advanced services with requirements of ultra-low latency and ultra-high reliability. How to make full use of the limited physical-layer resources is a key determinant to guarantee the quality of service (QoS). Therefore， resource allocation plays an essential role in exchanging information between vehicles， infrastructure， and other devices.In this Talk， we spotlight C-V2X in 5G cellular networks. In order to intelligently and reasonably allocate resources， we propose a self-adaptive fuzzy logic-based strategy. To evaluate the network performance for this adaptive strategy， a system model for C-V2X is built for urban areas， and typical safety and non-safety services are deployed in the network. Our results reveal that the proposed fuzzy logic-based algorithm can substantially improve resource utilization and satisfy the requirements of C-V2X， compared with prior counterparts， which cannot provide guaranteed services due to low resource utilization.
