等离子体来自古希腊语，1927年由美国化学家欧文朗缪尔描述为物质的第四种基本状态( 除了固态、气态和液态)。等离子体是最活跃、最丰富的物质状态，整个宇宙可见物质的99.9%以上都是由等离子体组成的。等离子体的独特地方就在于它是由基态和激发态的离子、电子和中性物质组成的气态物质。最近20年，大气压下冷(室温)等离子体(CAP)得到迅速的发展，在杀菌消毒、伤口愈合、美容、口腔、凝血、癌症治疗等展现出优良应用潜力，并形成一门 新的学科:等离子体医学。围绕着等离子体医学，重点介绍CAP肿瘤治疗、灭活冠状病毒以及等离子体医疗器械产业化。
1.At the core of complexity science， networked systems are ubiquitous across a broad range of fields from biology， neuroscience to society. The formation process of complex systems carries key information in extracting the systems' functional properties in relation to their topological structures. Here applying machine learning algorithms， we demonstrate for the first time that thehistorical formation process of various empirical networks can be extracted reliably with high precision， including protein-protein interaction， ecology， economic， and social networks. Specifically， our results show that the temporal link formation sequence of various complex networks can be recovered from the final network structure itself. Intriguingly， we discover that reliable restoration of network formation process can be achieved with only a little more information than random guess on pairwise order of links on large networks， meaning that history restora- tion is highly feasible on empirical networks. Furthermore， we find that recovering the historical formation processes reveals the underlying network evolution mechanisms. In addition to its fundamental scientific value， we further show that the recovered link temporal sequence significantly helps to enhance the performance of widely adopted link prediction algorithms， demonstrating its immense potential in practical applications.2.The genomes of multicellular organisms are extensively folded into 3D chromosome territories within the nucleus. It has been proposed that genome organization and function involve the interplay of proteins， RNAs， and chromatin architectures. So it is very important for developing 3D genome mapping methods to identify the structures and dynamic organization of the genome. Here we describe a strategy for investigating RNA-mediated chromatin DNA-DNA interactions (rDD). Using Epstein-Barr virus (EBV) immortalizes resting B-lymphocytes， we performed rDD assays to identify EBV noncoding RNAS mediated chromatin contactsbetween the virus and host. I will discuss our preliminary results and get feedback and ideas from the audience for further mining the data.
Despite the clinical success of targeted therapies directed towards driver oncogenes in many cancers， resistance to these therapies often emerges quickly， culminating in poor clinical outcomes. Although emerging evidence has revealed the crucial role of lineage plasticity in driving therapy resistance， the exact molecular mechanism and kinetics of acquiring lineage plasticity is not clearly understood. More importantly， therapeutic approaches targeting lineage plasticity-driven resistance are not currently available， underlying the unmet clinical urgency to identify druggable targets which drive lineage plasticity and resistance. Through a multi-disciplinary approach integrating 3D organoid modeling， bulk and single cell RNA-Seq (scRNA-Seq) analysis， we iluminate the once hidden intratumoral heterogeneous subclones， which express multilineage， stem-like， and lineage plastic transcriptional programs， as the driving force of AR therapy resistance. We reveal that the Janus kinase (JAK)-signal transducer and activator of transcription (STAT) signaling is a crucial executor in promoting lineage plasticity-driven AR targeted therapy resistance in prostate cancer. Importantly， ectopic JAK/STAT activation is specifically required for the resistance of stem-like subclones expressing multi-lineage transcriptional programs， but not subclones exclusively expressing the neuroendocrine (NE)-like lineage program. Both genetic and pharmaceutical inactivation of JAK-STAT signaling restored the AR dependency of prostate cancer cells or 3D-cutlured organoids and re- sensitized them to AR targeted therapy， giving hope that JAK-S TAT inhibitors could be a novel avenue to overcome resistance. Together， these data revealed the novel and crucial function of JAK-STAT signaling in promoting a stem-like and lineage plastic state and presented a novel therapeutic approach to reverse AR targeted therapy resistance using JAK1 inhibitor.
在试管婴儿(IVF)诊疗流程中，胚胎学家根据囊胚形态学分级选择最具存活能力的囊胚植入母体内，因此囊胚的评估和选择起着关键作用。囊胚形态学等级由囊胚的扩张程度以及内细胞团(ICM) 和滋养外胚层(TE)的质量所决定。近年来，各种基于深度学习和计算机视觉的方法被应用于囊胚图像质量的评估，这类方法可以降低人工成本并辅助临床决策支持。然而，以往的研究大多利用深度学习分类网络进行定性评估。在本次报告中，我们将介绍两种新型方法进行囊胚图像评估。第一，我们提出了一种结合软注意机制的回归网络来定量评价囊胚质量。该网络输出一一个连续的分数来精确地表示囊胚质量，而不再为分类等级。另外，注意力模块输出的激活图使网络决策更加可信。第二，我们提出了-种多模态表示学习框架，该框架首次利用囊胚的文本描述作为辅助监督信号，以丰富囊胚图像的视觉表征。对于这个特定的小数据集评级应用我们设计了一个双流网络，并引入了Vision Transformer作为图像编码器。此外，我们将囊胚评估问题重新定义为一个图像文本检索任务，以解决数据不均衡的问题。实验结果表明这两种方法为囊胚图像评估提供了有前景的解决方案。
辅助生殖技术(ART) 是人类不孕症治疗的有效方法，也是细胞与分子生物学、遗传学、生物工程、电子机械与信息科学、和药物学等多学科发展的体现。从细胞生物学的角度看，ART是精子和卵子结合、胚胎培养和筛选的单细胞操作技术;从分子生物学角度看，ART需要对精子、卵子、胚胎等细胞内大量分子改变、调控有充分理解;从遗传学角度看，ART涉及到单基因遗传病、线粒体遗传疾病，并要做出筛选;从生物工程角度看，ART需要3D培养环境、生物材料的帮助; ART对电子机械的精密器械有高水准的要求;辅助生殖激素亦对信息科学，特别是人工智能提出要求和期待。ART发展至今，面临诸多挑战。从生物学角度看，其中最大的挑战是卵子和精子老化、胚胎发育停滞、子宫内膜严重受损。生物学、电子机械学、信息科学等多学科的交叉会快速促进ART的发展。本次报告重点介绍是分子生物学、电子机械学科及信息科学特别是AI在ART研发中的机会。

微纳结构的有机/无机光电材料尺寸小，比表面积大，还有许多特殊和有趣的物理和化学特性，包括表面化学催化，量子限域效应，表面能带弯曲效应，亚波长光波导效应等。这些材料可以广泛地用来构建各种新型光电和化学传感器件。本报告将总结本课题组过去多年利用三维微纳多孔模板组装集成各种钙钛矿纳米线高效发光器件与光电检测器件。其中包括球形发光二极管(LED)，半球形仿生视网膜及球形仿生电子眼等器件等。另外，本报告还将介绍纳米结构的化学传感器以及高性能的智能电子鼻(E-nose)系统。该系统的核心为半导体氧化物纳米管传感器阵列，另外还有读出电路，无线数据传输单元及人工智能算法和移动数据处理应用程序。通过将独特的纳米管传感器结构与多种电极材料结合使用，实现了高灵敏度的气体检测和判别。因此，与使用薄膜的常规器件相比，大大降低了传感器的功耗，并且与同类进口产品相比有优越的灵敏度。这种传感器系统可以满足智能家居，智能建筑和智能城市中分布式环境监控的迫切需求，未来也可以用于移动与可穿戴设备。
Abscisic acid (ABA) is a critical phytohormone involved in multifaceted processes in plant metabolism and growth under both stressed and nonstressed conditions. Its accumulation in various tissues and cells has long been established as a biomarker for plant stress responses. To better understand ABA distribution and dynamics at subcellular resolution， we have developed a series of soluble and nanobody-based membrane-anchored ABA probes that are targeted to different sub-organelles. Using these organellar sensors， it was revealed that organellar ABA in different cells responded distinctly depending on environmental stimuli， Besides， we identified ABCG16 as a dual transporter in ABA signaling for mediating both cellular ABA efflux and ER entry of ABA- GE. FRET (Forster resonance energy transfer) analysis on the conformational status of ABCG16 dimers further disclosed specific alterations in the conformation of ABCG16 homo- and heterodimers in response to ABA and ABA-GE， respectively. Together， we provide a mechanistic framework for understanding substrate specificities that are linked to different endomembrane during ABCG transporter-mediated ABA homeostasis.
植物与其生活环境紧密接触，井持续接受外界信号和通过多种信号通路传递外界信号及做出合适的响应。信号转导系统存在一种本身不具备酶活性的蛋白质--支架蛋白(scaffold protein) ，它的作用类似分子胶水，将功能相关的蛋白粘合在一起，从而保证了信号传递的特异和高效。本报告将简要概述两类动植物保守的支架蛋自RACK1和14-3-3在植物信号转导的作用机制，以及描述我们最近两年的研究工作中发现的这两类支架蛋白在植物激素油菜素内酶BR信号传导中的交叉会话
We explore how information ambiguity and traders' attitudes toward ambiguity affect expectations and asset prices under three different market institutions. Specif- ically， we test the prediction of Epstein and Schneider (2008) that information ambiguity will lead market prices to overreact to bad news and to underreact to good news. We find that such an asymmetric reaction exists and is strongest in individ- ual prediction markets. It occurs to a lesser extent in single price call markets. It is weakest of all in double auction markets， where buyers' asymmetric reaction to good/bad news is cancelled out by the opposite asymmetric reaction of sellers.
Using a novel dataset based on individual resumes of public firm employees， we propose a monthly index of labor flows and decompose it into an expected level and unexpected shock component. We find that shocks strongly predict short-term market excess returns， while levels of labor hiring have insignificant forecasting power in the short run. The substantial return predictability of hiring shocks remains out of sample and delivers sizable economic value in asset allocation. Our findings cannot be explained by existing labor-related predictors and common economic variables. To exploit the underlying economic mechanism， we show that economic condition concerns are more likely to interpret the return predictability.
 An emerging subject in nonequilibrium physics is "order parameter steering" where experimentally controllable perturbations (e.g， light pulses) may drive the order parameters of symmetry broken phases to evolve in time. I will theoretically demonstrate this phenomenon in two cases: mean field steering and fluctuation steering. In the first case， we show that in excitonic insulators with 5-wave electron-hole pairing， an applied light pulse can induce a p-wave component to the order parameter， and further drive it to rotate in the s+ip plane. In one dimension， each cycle of rotation pumps exactly two electrons across the sample while higher dimensional systems are similar， realizing a Thouless charge pump as a collective manybody effect. In the second case， we study the dynamics of a competing order system which is rapidly heated up by a pump and then cooled down due to electron-lattice heat transfer. In the cooling process， exponentially growing thermal fluctuations lead the system into the phase associated with the faster-relaxing order parameter; which is not necessarily the ground state. This theory offers a natural explanation for the widespread experimental observation that metastable states may be induced by laser pulses.

根据定义，设计是一门以人类为中心的学科：提供消费品、支持产业、构建个人和集体生活方式。与工业和市场的联系使其成为支持现代社会寻求发展并将技术和创新与许多人的利益联系起来的学科。在人类中心主义的观点中，人类福祉被认为是技术创新和经济科学的目标。这带来了一个内在的矛盾：设计可能一直在支持巩固全球化发展理念中的消费主义社会，并且在很大程度上促成了我们面临的环境挑战。超越人类中心主义的界限讨论设计意味着同意：设计社会“已经荒谬地相信消费是解决我们作为一个物种的福祉的显而易见和合乎逻辑的方式”，并且“人类这一物种的福祉”包含的创造力和创新力是非常有限的。因此，我们如何看待超越人类的设计方法论？我们如何通过“过渡设计”来创造对所有生命形式的同理心？本次演讲将与各位分享关于如何消除文化与自然之间的区别的想法，进而支持一种新的设计实践，以重新发现生态纠缠，而非解决问题或设置问题。
珠绣的历史早在东汉以至隋唐、宋代均可见实物及文字记载。在广州东汉墓葬及广州晋、南朝墓葬中均出土过玻璃串珠等实物，其历史距今已有二千多年。粤绣(珠绣)源于中国工艺美术之都潮州，是粤绣的重要组成部分，是独具岭南特色的代表性传统工艺，还是一种十分精巧的手工刺绣艺术。珠绣创作者通常使用针线穿引珍珠。玻璃珠、宝石珠、珠片:晶石、胶石等多种材料，在画布或纺织品，花布、人造革、真皮等不同材料上绣出生动立体、色彩绚丽的图案。珠绣作品题材广泛，晶种繁多，既有壮丽豪华的巨型艺术作品和玲珑精巧的艺术品小件，又有兼具装饰性和实用性的珠绣毛衫。珠绣时装、珠绣玩具、珠绣腰带等日常生活用品。通过装饰性实用品及其在婚纱礼服。民间服饰。湖剧服饰中的广泛应用，珠绣得以广泛传播，现已扩展成为岭南文化的重要载体。本次讲座将从球绣的历史演变、材料:技艺、针法、门类等各方面讲述珠绣，赏析珠块面作品，领略珠绣所独有的动感与流光溢彩之美。
Nuclear Magnetic Resonance (NMR) is a very powerful experimental method that plays an important role in many fields such as physics， chemistry， materials， biology， medicine and earth sciences. To date， this technique has fostered five Nobel Prizes， In condensed matter physics， the physical properties of electron spin， orbit， charge， and lattice degrees of freedom in the surrounding chemical environment can be reflected according to the static and dynamic behavior of atomic ，nucleus degree of freedom， so it is a local and microscopic means of measurement. In this talk， I will briefly describe the principle of NMR technology and its applications in the fields of unconventional superconductivity， heavy fermion materials， quantum spin liquids， etc. Some examples will be given in terms of our recent progresses in strongly correlated materials like Sr2RuO4， CeNiAsO and YCu3(OH)6.5Br2.5.
With the trend of processing a large volume of sensitive data on PaaS services (e.g. DNN training)， a TEE architecture that supports general heterogeneous accelerators， enables spatial sharing on one accelerator， and enforces strong isolation across accelerators is highly desirable. However， none of the existing TEE solutions meet all three requirements. In this paper， we propose CRONUS， the first TEE architecture that achieves the three crucial requirements. The key idea of CRONUS is to partition heterogeneous computation into isolated TEE enclaves， where each enclave encapsulates only one kind of computation (e.g. GPU computation)， and multiple enclaves can spatially share an accelerator. Then， CRONUS constructs heterogeneous computing using remote procedure calls (RPCs) among enclaves. With CRONUS， each accelerator' s hardware and its software stack are strongly isolated from others' ，and each enclave trusts only its own hardware. To tackle the security challenge caused by inter-enclave interactions， we design a new streaming remote procedure call abstraction to enable secure RPCs with high performance. CRONUS is softwarebased， making it general to diverse accelerators. We implemented CRONUS on ARM TrustZone. Evaluation on diverse workloads with CPUs， GPUs and NPUs shows that， CRONUS achieves less than 7.1% extra computation time compared to native (unprotected) executions.
We argue that， despite the spectacular achievements of machine learning techniques， we are still far from Artificial General Intelligence (AGl). A big step toward this goal would be to develop autonomous systems capable of replacing human agents working in complex organizations， as envisioned by the loT. This requires in particular， the convergence between Computing and Al integrating data-based machine learning and model-based systems engineering. We discuss the relevance of existing criteria for comparing human and machine intelligence and show some notable analogies and differences between scientific knowledge and that produced by neural networks.Emphasizing that autonomy is an important step towards AGI， we present a characterization of autonomous systems， and show key differences with mental systems equipped with common sense knowledge and reasoning.We conclude by advocating challenging work directions， including the development of a new foundation for systems engineering and scientific knowledge， and the joint exploration of physical and mental phenomena that embody human intelligence.
本次报告将主要介绍雷晓光课题组如何利用化学遗传学手段深入探索与人类重大疾病紧密联系的程序性细胞死亡的分子机制，进而利用化学生物学、药物化学、结构生物学等研究手段，发现新的药物靶标与开发创新型小分子候选药物。
To delineate molecular machines with atomic detail inside cells Represents the future of tructural biology. With cryo-electron tomography（crVO-ET）and advanced sub-tomogram analysis，determined the ribosome average at 3.0A resolution inside Mycoplasma pneumoniae cells. Extensive sub-tomogram classification of ribosomes in native cells determined more than 13 intermediate structures (4-10 A resolutions） along active translation， which not only visualizes the structural dynamics but also provides unique insights into their functional landscapes inside cells. Mapping back the classified ribosomes into the tomogram reveals the spatial and functionalorganization of translating ribosomes in the cell which unraveled a local coordination mechanism within polysomes that is mediated by the ribosomal protein L9. Moreover a variety of supramolecular assemblies formed by ribosomes and other molecular machines were captured， which include transcription-translation coupling complexes， ribosome-translocon complexes， and other supercomplexes that may only form within the cellular context. Furthermore， I resolved more than 17 ribosome intermediate structures in three different antibiotic-treated datasets，and demonstrated how the drug molecules drastically reshape structural and functional landscapes of the translation machinery inside bacterial cells. The works pushed limits of cryo-ET and sub-tomogram analysis， and herald a new era of integrative in-cell structural biology.
Existing popular Blockchain consensus mechanisms ，such as Proof-of-Work (PoW）， are designed to record existing transactions. However， they play no role in the transaction generation process. Many blockchain applications require high computation costs to generate and record transactions (e.g， in the case of PoW）. In this paper， we propose an approach that allows us to utilize the consensus generation process to generate transactions by solving complex problems. We call it the Proof-of-Merit (PoM） mechanism-this approach decentralizes the transaction-generation process and selects proposed solutions to the problem based on their merit. We illustrate the PoM mechanism in thee context of ridesharing， where a group of solvers provide solutions to the problem of matching riders with drivers. Moreover， we define two objectives-efficiency and equity-to evaluate：PoM. We demonstrate PoMs performance and nuanced properties using agent-based simulation. We show how Decentralized Control Parameter(DCP） influences the intrinsic tradeoffs between efficiency and equity. Further ， we explore how to find the proper value of DCP towards achieving a desirable balance of the two objectives.

Beam exposure and target lifetime.The top JUNA performance help the research team to deliver precision nuclear astrophysics rection rates that rule out the nuclear physics uncertainties including space gamma emission， neutron source in star and overabundance of Ca in coldest stars observed by JWST. The research result was published PRL and Nature and was invited to keynote talk inrecent APPC 15 conferences.The research highlights of JUNA will be presented.
This study examines how minimum wage hikes affect firms industrial pollution. Using the establishment-level pollutant emission data on Chinese industrial firms and exploring the minimum wage policy discontinuities at county borders ， we find that minimum wage hikes induce firms to pollute more and reduce their abatement efforts. In particular， a 10% increase inminimum wage corresponds to a 4.63% increase in COD emissions .State ownership mitigates the negative impact of minimum wages on pollutant emissions， suggesting its role in addressing externality. The effects of minimum wages on pollutant emissions are stronger for financially constrained firms and firms with lower product market power，and higher labor intensity. These effects are attenuated with the staggered increase of pollution fee charges across provinces. Overall，our findings highlight the unintended environmental consequences of labor market policies.
Correlation functions and entanglement are two different aspects to characterize quantum many-body states. While many correlation functions are experimentally accessible， entanglement entropy(EE)， the simplest characterization of quantum entanglement， is usually difficult to measure. In this talk， I will introduce a protocol to bound EE by local measurements.This protocol untilizes local correlation matrices and focuses on their (approximate) zero eigenvalues. Given a quantum state， each (approximate) zero eigenvalue can be used to define a set of local projection operators.An auxiliary Hamiltonian can then be constructed by summing these projuctors. When the construction only involves projectors of zero eigenvlaues， we prive the EE of a subsystem is bounded by the ground-state degeneracy of the anxiliary Hamiltonian on this subsysterm.When projectors from nonzero eigenvalues are included， we show the EE can be bounded by a thermal entropy of the subsystem.Our protocol can be applied experimentally to investgate exotic quantum many-body states prepared in quantum simulators.
产品站设计是小米生态链爆品打造过程中必不可少的重要一环，是小米在众多智能硬件科技品牌/公司脱颖而出的制胜法宝，它运用消费者用户最通俗易懂且注重参与感的文案表达、配以极简精致、品质舒适的页面图素设计，结合创意营销深度推广小米/米家智能产品来获得用户的极致口碑传播。我将为大家介绍和分享关于如何在复杂多变的商业营销环境下，通过提升产品视觉传达设计，实现美学风格鲜明独特的产品表达，让产品设计持续在「体验与美」价值升华的同时，帮助用户解决更多现实痛点问题，向往更美好的生活。
Traditional Peking opera performers did not use musical notation in their performances and training. Many were illiterate， and very few could read gongche notation (a traditional Chinese musical notation). While training， they emulated melodies performed orally by their masters， memorized tunes， and improvised onstage. However， after the founding of the People’s Republic of China， cipher notation was introduced as an ‘advanced’ tool for teaching and preserving Peking opera at theatre schools. In contrast， gongche notation came to be regarded as ‘outdated.’ Later， the rise of professional composers and the compiling of Peking opera teaching materials accelerated the popularization of cipher notation. Nowadays， the younger generation of Peking opera practitioners heavily depends on musical notation， directly resulting in the rapid decline of improvised performances onstage.Nevertheless， the wide use of cipher notation has significantly contributed to the teaching and preservation of Peking opera music. By taking qinshi (the lead accompanist who plays the Peking opera fiddle jinghu) and their accompaniments as examples， this talk examines the historical background of using cipher notation at theatre schools， different beat conceptions (the one in the cipher notation and that in the Peking opera rhythmic system)， and qinshi’s opinions towards using musical notations. I argue that influenced by Westernized ideas promoted during the New Culture Movement， cipher notation was regarded as superior to gongche notation. Yet， nowadays， qinshi do not consider cipher notation a perfect notation. The debates on whether to use musical notation reflect contemporary qinshi’s reflective thinking on balancing jinghu accompaniment traditions and challenges they’ve encountered in their jinghu accompaniments.
智能纺织品的可编程特性使其成为新兴新技术领域不可或缺的一部分。结合微电子学和能源、人工智能、纺织微电子异质集成等技术，智能近身可穿戴系统得到了广泛关注和深入探索。智能纺织集成微电子智能可穿戴系统在医疗保健、体育、教育、保护和虚拟世界中得到越来越多的应用。本报告介绍了我们团队在近身智能可穿戴系统的三类关键平台技术的最新研究工作进展。包括 (1) 自主研发的微电子纺织系统异质集成技术，设计、制造、测试嵌入式微电子芯片的电子纱线和织物器件和系统。（2）高输出纤维基直流发电机的机理研究、材料设计与合成、装置设计、制备、测试和应用。（3）智能可穿戴系统的设计、制备、建模和测试评估以及增强帕金森病患者活动能力的应用实例。

化学生物学（Chemical biology）作为一门新兴的交叉学科，通过运用化学小分子作为工具研究生物学问题，在人类疾病研究和药物开发过程中发挥了巨大作用。化学遗传学（Chemical genetics）作为经典遗传学的补充，借助小分子化合物实现对蛋白家族的广谱或特异调控，具有时间和空间上的灵活性，克服经典遗传学面临的基因冗余和突变致死等瓶颈。近年，化学遗传学在植物科学特别是植物激素信号转导机制研究中得到广泛应用。本次报告将简要概述化学生物学在生长素研究中的应用，并以我们近期开发的生长素酰胺合成酶GRETCHEN HAGEN3（GH3）的小分子抑制剂为例介绍化学调控剂开发的研究方法和策略。

以往的水合物热激法解析模型往往只关注水合物分解过程中的传热和渗流特征，却忽视了其中的地质力学效应。然而，在热激法下的水合物分解同样是一个多物理场耦合的过程，地质力学效应不应被忽略。因此我们基于已有的解析模型建立了一个考虑地质力学效应的水合物热激法热流固耦合模型，并且采用增量法实现了对耦合系统的求解。我们验证了模型的可靠性并且对比了Lagrange’s孔隙度和真实孔隙度对耦合系统的影响。结果显示，在小应变假设下，不同孔隙度策略造成的误差对于耦合系统的影响比较小，可以接受。随后，我们基于该模型和求解方法展开了参数分析，计算了应力荷载、边界温度和边界压力对于耦合系统的影响。与此前模型相比，我们的模型更加全面，并且可以揭示水合物储层在热激作用下的更多特征。

Checkpoint inhibiting drugs targeting the PD1 pathway represent one of the most encouraging new therapeutics for cancer. Millions of cancer patients have benefited from using checkpoint inhibitors since their first approval in 2014 by the US FDA. However ， most cancer patients do not respond to PD1 pathway inhibitors and those who do eventually develop disease progression. Therefore，there is a strong unmet need to improve the efficacy of PD1 pathway inhibitors or todevelop drugs targeting new immune checkpoint regulators. In this talk，Dr.Chen will discuss new developments in the field of immune checkpoint research and new opportunities for developing the next class of anti-cancer immunotherapeutic drugs.

Achieving desirable building performance is an important objective of architectural design but is often regarded as an "obstacle" to creativity. By considering the performance issues at the early design stage， they may become inspirations for design， especially with the help of computational design methods. In this seminar， three studies investigating how building science can be turned into inspirations for design are reported.A computational design framework and tool helping architects design auditoriums with acoustic requirements as the driving factor;Geometry optimization of acoustic retroreflectors to boost voice support for outdoor spaces;Design experiments examining the effectiveness of a real-time feedback tool in improving building performance and exciting design innovations.
This talk will describe how fuzzy transfer learning can innovatively and effectively learn from data to support data-driven decision-making in uncertain and dynamic situations. The core idea behind fuzzy transfer learning is to leverage previously acquired knowledge to assist in completing a prediction task in a related domain by integrating fuzzy techniques with the transfer  learning process. A set of new fuzzy transfer learning theories，methodologies，and algorithms is introduced，which transfers knowledge learned in one or more source domains to target domains. The fuzzy transfer learning set incorporates:(1)a fuzzy refinement domain adaptation algorithm by utilizing the fuzzy system and similarity/dissimilarity concepts to modify the target instances labels for classification;(2) fuzzy rule-based systems with mapping functions by building latent spaces to facilitate knowledge transfer for regression tasks in both homogeneous and heterogeneous scenarios;(3)unsupervised domain adaptation， to recognize newly emerged patterns in target domains that may be unlabeled. Patterns in target domains and solutions to heterogeneous unsupervised domain adaptation via e.g.， fuzzy equivalence relations. These new developments can enhance date-driven prediction and decision support systems in complex real-world environments. Applications of transfer learning will be discussed at the end.

随着深度神经网络在各个领域的广泛应用，DNN的质量问题也得到了学界和业绩的广泛关注。深度神经网络测试是保证DNN质量的最常用方法之一。深度神经网络测试常常需要将大量带有标注的测试用例输入到DNN模型，并将DNN模型的预测结果与已标注的标签进行比较以检查DNN的准确性。然而标注测试用例往往通过引入大量人力成本，这为DNN测试带来了巨大的开销，对整体测试效率造成影响。为了缓解标注开销的问题，本报告介绍一种新的测试用例排序方法 PRIMA，通过智能变异分析寻找更能揭错的测试输入并在有限的时间内优先进行标注，以提升DNN 测试的效率。

Inactivation of the RB1 tumor suppressor gene is common in several types of therapy-resistant cancers， including metastatic castration-resistant prostate cancer， and predicts poor clinical outcomes. Effective therapeutic strategies against RB1-deficient cancers， however， remain elusive. In this presentation，we show that RB1-loss/E2F activation sensitizes cancer cells to ferroptosis，a form of regulated cell death driven by iron-dependent lipid peroxidation by upregulating expression of ACSL4 and enriching ACSL4-dependent arachidonic acid-containing phospholipids ， which are key components of ferroptosis execution. ACSL4 appears to be a direct E2F target gene and is critical to RB1 loss-induced sensitization to ferroptosis. Importantly. using cell line-derived xenografts and genetically engineered tumor models，we demonstrate that induction of ferroptosis in vivo by JKE-1.674， a highly selective and stable GPX4 inhibitor， blocks RB1-deficient prostate tumor growth and metastasis and leads to improved survival of the mice. Thus， our Findings uncover an RB/E2F/ACSL4 molecular axis that governs ferroptosis， and also Suggest a new approach to the treatment of RB1-deficient malignancies.

We propose a new concept， oblivious quantum computation，which requires performing oblivious transfer with respect to the computation outcome of the quantum computation ， where the secrecy 0f the input qubits and the program to identify the quantum gates are required. We propose a two-server protocol for this task，which realizes an exponential improvement for the communication complexity over the simple application of two-Server（quantum）oblivious transfer to the sending of the computation result. AIso，We propose another new concept delegated multiparty quantum computation，in which， several users ask multiparty quantum computation to server(s) only using classical communications. We propose a two-server protocol for the latter task as well. This talk is based on the latest arXiy paper: http://arxiv.org/abs/2211.00962.
Motivated by geometric Langlands， we initiate a program to study the mirror symmetry between nilpotent orbit closures of a semisimple Lie algebra and those of its Langlands dual.The most interesting case is Bn via Cn. Classically， there is a famous Springer duality between special orbits. Therefore， it is natural to speculate that the mirror symmetry we seek may coincide with Springer duality in the context of special orbits. Unfortunately， such a naive statement fails. To remedy the situation， we propose a conjecture which asserts the mirror symmetry for certain parabolic/induced covers of special orbits. Then， we prove the conjecture for Richardson orbits and obtain certain partial results in general. In the process， we reveal some very interesting and yet subtle structures of these finite covers， which are related to Lusztig’s canonical quotients of special nilpotent orbits. For example， there is a mysterious asymmetry in the footprint or range of degrees of these finite covers. Finally， we provide two examples to show that the mirror symmetry fails outside the footprint.This is a joint work with Yongbin Ruan and Yaoxiong Wen.
Gravitational instantons are the building blocks of Hawking's quantum gravity theory. They are non-compact hyperK\ahler 4-manifolds with L^2 curvature and can be viewed as the local pieces of K3 surfaces. Similar to K3 surfaces， the cohomology classes of the hyperK\"ahler triples of gravitational instantons induce a period map. In this talk， we will restrict to a particular type of gravitational instanton of type ALH^*. As a side product of studying SYZ mirror symmetry of log Calabi-Yau surfaces， we will prove that the period map is both injective and surjective. As a consequence， the period domain is the moduli space of ALH^*-gravitational instantons. The talk is based on joint works with T. Collins， A. Jacob and the joint work with T.-J. Lee."
真核生物中具有染色质重塑因子能够与辅助亚基结合形成多亚基复合体，介导核小体的组装、去除、移位以及组蛋白变体的置换等过程。以往植物中的研究发现了许多染色质重塑复合体的保守组分，并研究了它们的生物学功能然而缺乏对植物染色质重塑复合体的系统研究，这限制了我们对植物染色质重塑复合体功能的理解。我们系统鉴定了植物中的ISWI，SWR1，INO80及SWI/SNF等几种重要染色质重塑复合体的亚基组成，发现了染色质重塑复合体的多个植物特异亚基，揭示了植物染色质重塑与其他染色质修饰独特的偶联机制。这些研究为进一步探索植物中染色质重塑的生物学功能和分了机制奠定了基础。

Successful implementation of quantum information processing applications requires achieving robust qubits that are well protected from the environmental noise. As such，spectral characterization of noise environments that lead to the decoherehce of qubits is critical for quantum hardware design. Over the past decade，various dynamical decoupling-based methods were designed for characterization of the noise spectra. However these approaches come at the cost of applying large or complex squences of pulses. In this talk， l will go over the developments of the field， and introduce a novel noise spectroscopy method that utilizes only the Fourier transform of free induction decay measurements. This mathod faithfully recovers the correct noise spectra and outperforms the current dynamical decoupling schemes while significantly reduces the experimental overhead. I also discuss the experimental feasibility of this method with respect to reguiring fast pulses. In particular， I will present a quantum control method for achieving extremely fast pulses in optically active systems（such as Quantum dots and color centers)， while avoiding the leakage to the nearby unwanted states. The presented methods are applicable to a wide range of quantum platforms and provide a more practical path towards a more accurate spectral characterization and control of quantum platforms.

古菌是第三种生命形式，与细菌及真核生物并列的三大生物域之一。古菌不仅称霸高温热泉、深海热液口等极端环境，更广泛存在子于海洋、湿地和动物肠道等温和环境。古菌适应极端环境变化的法宝之一是它们拥有独树一职的单分子层细胞膜脂类结构-一四醚脂类GDGTs。我们通过古菌遗传学方法，首次发现一系列古菌GDGTs合成酶基因，闸明它们的表达调控机制，最终揭示GDGTs响应不同环境变化的生理功能，古菌GDGTs的研究有助于我们认识生命适应极端环境的机制，早期生命起源演化过程，乃至于地球古环境古气候变迁的历史。
植物的生长发育过程不仅受到内部发育信号如激素的调控，也受到外界信号如光和逆境信号等的调节，因此植物如何整合内外信号进而调控生长发育是一个有趣且重要的科学问题。本次报告将以FTIP（FT-Interacting Proteins）家族蛋白为切入点，汇报FTIPS介导互作蛋白的运输、互作蛋白与其互作因子如何协同调控靶基因进而调控水稻生长发育的分子机制：如通过影响激素合成调控水稻育性和参与成花素转运调控水稻抽穗期的机理；调节水稻高效合理应答非生物胁迫以保证胁迫应答和生长发育之间的能量平衡分配的机制。还将进一步展望该家族蛋白与其互作蛋白在植物适应性和产量方面的作用。

We present an effective BV quantization theory for chiral deformation of two dimensional conformal field theories. We explain a connection between the quantum master equation and the chiral homology for vertex operator algebras. As an application， we construct correlation functions of the curved beta-gamma/b-c system and establish a coupled equation relating to chiral homology groups of chiral differential operators. This can be viewed as the vertex algebra analogue of the trace map in algebraic index theory. The talk is based on the recent work arXiv:2112.14572 [math.QA].
Hitchin’s integrable systems lie in the crossroads of geometry， representation theory， and mathematical physics. I will discuss two central conjectures raised in the last two decades which greatly influenced the development for the algebraic geometry of Hitchin moduli spaces. The first is the P=W conjecture， which concerns the interaction of the topology of the Hitchin system and the non-abelian Hodge correspondence. The second is the topological mirror symmetry conjecture which connects the Langlands duality of groups and the mirror symmetry for Hitchin systems. I will explain that both conjectures can be proved in a uniform way， via vanishing cycles techniques and support theorem. Based on joint work with Davesh Maulik.
在虚拟现实（VR）系统中，用户可查看虚拟内容并与之交互，其中，虚拟对象的选择和操控是VR环境中两个重要的基本任务。与更传统的平台相比，VR场景中的交互不够精确和高效，需要付出更多的工作量。我将介绍在VR场景中如何有效地选择和操控虚拟对象的技术设计方向的最新工作。首先讨论如何利用用户行为信息来开发优化的对象选择技术；然后介绍我们如何使用隐性信息，例如眼睛注视数据和手持控制器来补充和增强对象操纵；最后介绍最新的在VR场景中，如何有效地进行多用户操纵对象组的交互研究。

In this talk，the cooperative output regulation problem for heterogeneous linear multi-agent systems with jointly connected directed communication topologies via event-triggered control protocol will be presented. First，the event-triggered control approach will be briefly reviewed. Then for the considered systems，a distributed event-triggered control strategy is proposed todeal with the jointly connected digraphs. With this control strategy，the tracking error of the closed-loop system converges to zero exponentially with intermittent communication. The continuous monitoring issue is also solved. Moreover， Zeno behavior can be avoided by providing a positive minimum inter-event time.
With an increasing human population， medical research is pushed to progress into an era of precision therapy，Through adoptive transfer of human stem cells into immunodeficient mice，we have established various humanized mouse models，with stable human blood， liver and other biological systems. These humanised mice are at the very heart of this new forefront where it is acutely required to decipher human-specific disease pathogenesis and test an array of novel therapeutics.Our humanized mouse models have been used to successfully support the in vivo studies of many human diseases including infectious pathogens， cancers， metabolic diseases and autoimmune diseases and closely recapitulate disease pathogenesis and drug mechanisms in humans. This presentation will focus on the background of humanised mice， disease modelling and human-specific mechanisms and therapeutics tested on this platform for future clinical use.
The cart-pole system is a benchmark example for both classical nonlinear control design and reinforcement learning. The challenge involves two steps: 1）swinging up the pole to the upward position and 2）balancing the pole in the upward position while bringing the cart position back to its initial position. In this talk， I will discuss this control problem with two purposes. Firstly，l will provide a theoretically provable nonlinear controller for the system under the assumption that the system model is available. Secondly，I will then study model-free control design but with the assumption that the system structure is known.This will be compared with the reinforcement learning approach in terms of both control performance and learning complexities. I will also take this opportunity to introduce some other research works of mine ，with the purpose of seeking collaborations. In particular，I will discusss briefly a recent work on ultra high precision tracking with potential applications in nano-scale image scanning and super resolution resonance generation.

Conventional lithium-ion batteries(LiBs)， which revolutionized the mobile electronics industry ，are widely used in daily life. However， the rapidly growing application of LIBs has raised concerns regarding their energy density limit and potential safety risks caused by the flammable organic liquid electrolytes. All-solid-state lithium batteries (ASSLBs) utilizing solid-stateel ectrolytes(ssEs) not only possess enhanced safety but may also offer new opportunities for the utilization of high-voltage cathode materials and high-capacity electrodes to achieve high-energy-density batteries. In addition，ASSLBs also possess further advantages including SSEs with high Li+ transfer efficiency， simple battery design，and a wide range of operating temperature. Nevertheless， ASSLBs still have challenges such as limited ionic conductivity and interface issues，So we will talk about the challenges and opportunities of all-solid-state batteries in this report.
质谱技术由于具有灵敏度高、样品用量少、检测速度快等优点被广泛应用于化学化工、环境能源、医药、生命及材料科学等领域。该讲座将介绍质谱技术的基本原理及其应用、实验室提供的各项测试服务及应用举例。
I will discuss the oscillatory integrals on the mirror Landau-Ginzburg models for toric mirrors. They are related to genus zero Gromov-Witten invariants and are compatible with homological mirror symmetry. The asymptotic expansion of such integrals leads to the Gamma II conjecture for toric varieties. I will also report some recent progress in some non-toric situation inspired by the Gross-Siebert program.
Inside a symplectic leaf of the cluster Poisson variety of Borel-decorated $PGL_2$ local systems on a punctured surface is an isotropic subvariety we will call the “chromatic Lagrangian.” Local charts for the quantized cluster variety are quantum tori defined by cubic planar graphs， and can be put in standard form after some additional markings giving the notion of a “framed seed.” The mutation structure is encoded as a groupoid. The local description of the chromatic Lagrangian defines a “wavefunction” which， we conjecture， encodes open Gromov-Witten invariants of a Lagrangian threefold in threespace defined by the cubic graph and the other data of the framed seed. We also find a relationship we call “framing duality”: for a family of “canoe” graphs， wavefunctions for different framings encode DT invariants of symmetric quivers.This talk is based on joint work with Gus Schrader and Linhui Shen.

The Bistrizer-MacDonald(BM) model predicted the existence of the narrow bands in the magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG)， and nowadays is a starting point for most theoretical works. In this talk， I will briefly review the BM model and then present the derivation of a continuum field theory [1] based on a microscopic tight binding model allowing arbitrary smooth lattice deformation including the small twist angle. With the gradient expansion to the second order， the continuum thoery for MATBG[2] produces the spectrum that almost perfectly matches the spectrum of the spectrum of the microscopic model，suggesting the validity of this theory. In the presence of the lattice deformation， the inclusion of the pseudo-vector potential does not destroy but shift the flat band chiral limit to a smaller twist angle. Furthermore， the continuum theory contains another important interlayer tunneling term that was overlooked in all previous works. This term non-negligibly breaks the particle-hole symmetry of the narrow bands and may be related with the experimentally observed particle-hole asymmetry. 
1.Memory interference is a common cause of forgetfulness. The hippocampus is the core brain region of memory. Dentate gyrus is the first step of information transfer into the hippocampus. Theoretical models have predicted a crucial role for the dentate gyrus in pattern separation，aprocess that reduces overlapping of inputs and enhances dissimilarity between representations and thus avoid memory interference. We aimed to investigate the place field properties of different cell types of dentate gyrus and their roles in pattern separation. We also investigated the physiological properties of hippocampal CA1 neurons as a consequence of dentate gyrus loss of function. We used tetrode recording，as well as juxtacellular labeling and recording in freely moving rats to distinguish different cell types in dentate gyrus. Utilizing a mouse line lacking dentate gyrus，we performed microendoscopic calcium imaging in CAl to examine the function of dentate gyrus on CA1.Our data suggest that different cell types in dentate gyrus performed pattern separation using different mechanisms and dentate gyrus was necessary for the CA1 neurons to accurately represent spatial locations.2.Understanding the relationship between Cancer cell proliferation and tumor microenvironment is highly challenging using in vivo bioimaging techniques. The applicant's research interests focus on the molecular design of optical imaging probes，which can label and track the tumor cells and other cells (eg.，immune cells mesenchymal stem cells) for long-term in vivo imaging studies. Wehave explored a series of exogenous cell trackers with optimized optical properties. Especially. the intrinsic signal dilution effect of traditional exogenous optical trackers has been surmounted to ensure long-term in vivo tracking of tumor growth. With the aid of multimodality fluorescent and photoacoustic probes，the dynamic migration of immune cells(e.g.，macrophages)in disease microenvironment can be analyzed using across- platform imaging approach. In future，we plan to develop optical probes that are capable of regulating the tumor microenvironment and elucidate the changes of cell-cell interaction during these biological processes.
相比于传统智能设备，新型智能设备在形态、功能、尺型、硬件组成等方面具有独特属性，这既给用户情境信息的挖掘带来了机遇，也为面向新型设备交互技术带来了挑战。一方面，由于新型智能设备的类型和所内置传感器的种类要丰富得多且其与用户更加切近能够获取到用户更为深层次的情境信息。因此，有必要研究面向新型智能终端的高效交互技术，主要解决装载传感器种类、数量的限制与交互需求之间的矛盾，以及算力、能量与实时精细交互之间的矛盾。

光刻是集成电路制造中的核心工艺，它负责把设计图形高保真地转移到硅片上，光刻工艺占据了芯片制造总成本的1/3以上。先进光刻工艺是由设备、材料和软件支撑的。光刻机负责对准和曝光，匀胶显影机负责涂胶和噪光后的显影。光刻胶和显影液负责把曝光时的空间像转换成光刻胶图形。电镜和套刻误差测量设备负责对硅片上得到的图形质量进行最后的监测。设计图形必须经过计算光刻软件处理后才可以被制备到拖模版上用于曝光，同时，拖模版图必须与光刻机的噪光方式协同才可以得到最佳的分辨率。本报告介绍集成电路先进光刻（14nm及以下技术节点）中使用的设备、材料与软件，以及它们之间是如何协同优化的。
With rapid progress in fabrication and control ， the coherent time of artificial quantum systems such as ultracold atoms and superconducting circuits has been improved significantly which makes them possible to explore exotic quantum dynamical behavior. In this talk， I present our recent work on achieving a new topological phase of matter in quasiperiodically driven systems. The new QFTEP can be oxperimentally realized in one-dimensional fermionic systems with two incommensurate driven freguencies， and is characterized by topologically protected quantized energy transport between the inommensurate driving modes. For a compactly occoupied fermionic chain the energy transport is achieved by absorbing a photon at one end and emitting anothor photon with the Second frequency at the other end. Such a non-trivial topological phase requires localization in both frequeney and spatial domains which means a moderate amount of spatial disorder will be in favor of the formation oF QFTEP. The effect oF interactions is discussed briefly: it is slhown numerically that QFTEP wil probably survive over weak interactions: As an alternative to observe the new topological phase， a primitive model of a two-level system driven by three mutually incommensurate frequencies is presented at last.
To understand molecular mechanisms of cellular pathways， contemporary workflows typically require multiple techniques to identify proteins，track their localization， and determine their structures in vitro. Here， we developed a visual proteomics approach to address these questions and understand how mammalian sperm are built. Our in situ cryo-electron tomography and subtomogram averaging provided 6.0 A reconstructions of axonemal microtubule structures. The well-resolved tertiary structures allowed us to computationally match， in an unbiased mannner，novel densities with 21，615 AlphaFold-predicted protein models of the mouse proteome. We identified novel sperm proteins that form an extensive interaction network crosslinking the lumen of microtubules， suggesting roles in modulating the mechanical properties of the microtubule filaments during flagellar beating.
As the first excavated ancient copper mining and smelting site in China， the Tonglushan site is highly evaluated by academia as one fundamental copper resource of the Chinese Bronze Age civilization. In this view， the site is regarded as the birthplace of Chinese bronze technology by the local government and is aimed to be titled a World Heritage.Based on one-year fieldwork at Daye county， China， this talk intends to present the negotiations behind the heritagisation process of Tonglushan. Specifically， to figure out the uniqueness of this mineral-based heritage place， the speaker investigates how the UNESCO concept of heritage practice at one Chinese archaeological site. In what ways do the authorized stakeholders interpret the site with national significance and universal value? And what have they met during the application of this interpretation? The concept of “heritage” itself and the inhabitants’ local knowledge and memory of the place will be the main focuses.
椭偏仪设备由于检测速度快，精度较高，广泛应用于材料学、微电子、光学、化学等相关领域，测量材料的光学泪关参数以及薄膜膜厚。本次主要介绍椭偏仪设备的发展、设备原理及样品测试条件、工作范围等，并且简要介绍椭偏仪建模基础及部分案例。
非酒精性脂肪肝疾病（NAFLD）包括脂肪肝和更为严重的肝脏疾病如非酒精性脂肌性肝炎（NASH），肝硬化等。NAFLD向NASH的发展可以诱发多种疾病如肝硬化，肝癌以及心血管疾病等，但其机制仍不十分清楚。我们利用组织特异性的基因敲除小鼠和细胞，结合RNAseq等生物信息学方法，并通过细胞生物学和生物化学等实验，证实了新近发现的cGAS/STING免疫信号通路通过调控巨噬细胞吞噬功能，在NASH的发生发展过程中起着非常重要的作用。此外我们发现肝脏中的巨噬细胞是一把双刃剑，对于肝脏损伤修复和维持肝脏稳态至关重要。我们的研究不仅阐明了cGAS调控巨噬细胞吞噬功能的机制，也为治疗NASH等肝脏疾病提任了新的药物靶点。

Deep learning has achieved impressive successes in a wide range of applications and has been applied in many branches of scientific research. In this talk，we provide a review of basic deep learning methodology and algorithms and present several recently developed learning methods from a statistical perspective，focusing on deep generative learning，semi-supervised learning，and representation learning. We then discuss applications of these methods to biomedical data  analysis， including analysis of medical imaging，electronic health record，and single-cell genomics data.
We examine the relationship between audit quality and audit-office level individual auditor turnover in the U.S.Using resumes of over 140，000 auditors from Indeed.com and Linkedin we find that audit offices with higher turnover have a greater likelihood of annual report restatements by clients，and are more likely to fail to detect material weakness in clients' internal controls over financial reporting. The detrimental effect of auditor turnover is mainly attributable to the departure of auditors with 4-8 years' experience，and is more pronounced for less important clients， for engagements with long auditor tenure and for large offices. Our results are robust to using outside job opportunities as an instrument variable and alternative measures of audit quality. Our findings directly inform the current policy debate initiated by the PCAOB on whether disclosures of audit quality indicators， particularly auditor turnover ， will help investors better evaluate audit guality.
笼目晶格本征携带狄拉克费米子、电子平带和范霍夫奇点。狄拉克电子引入了能带拓扑；电子平带助长了磁性涨落；范霍夫奇点则带来了长程电子序。它们在量子层次的共同作用引发了一系列拓扑笼目磁体和超导体的发现。我将讨论该领域的发现与发展，包括笼目晶体电子结构的基本概念，陈数磁体和外尔磁体的发现，多种形式的平带多体关联，电荷密度波以及超导态的谜团。我将阐述最新发现与原始概念的联系，笼目磁体与笼目超导体的联系，以及它们和拓扑绝绿体、外尔半金属、高温超导的联系。该领域的进展广泛地连接了量子霍尔和多体关联物理，并深刻地拓展了量子演生前沿。

互联网学习是指学生在互联网构建的灵活时空中，利用数字化资源与工具开展学习活动来实现知识、技能与态度等方面的发展。数字素养是个体为适应数字环境与全面参与社会生活所必须具备的能力。在互联网学习情境下，提升学习者的数字素养有助于其有效利用学习环境中的资源与工具，从而提升自身的互联网学习质量。然而，在互联网学习情境下发展数字素养面临两个关键的问题。其一，不断涌现的数字素养定义与框架加剧了数字素养概念的模糊性，引发了实践者的诸多困惑。其二，面向互联网学习的数字素养缺乏专门的评估框架与测量工具，无法为实践提供足够支持。本研究一方面基于典型的数字素养框架，深入辨析了数字素养的概念与特征；另一方面结合互联网学习情境特征，构建了面向该情境的数字素养框架，并开发了相应的评估工具，以此为相关实践提供支持。

Plant roots associate with diverse microbes (bacteria，fungi，and viruses） collectively called the rhizosphere microbiome， Among them，mycorrhizal fungi and rhizobia colonize host roots and Improve their access to nutrients， phosphorus and nitrogen. My research focus on the genetics， biochemistry and cell biology of two symbiotic interactions of plants that can help to achieve higher crop yields with less usage of fertilizers: One is the arbuscular mycorrhizal association that helps the host plant to uptake nutrients from the soil and is especially important for plant acquisition of phosphate and nitrogen. The other is the rhizobial symbiosis that provides a source of nitrogen to the host plant.In addition，we propose to transfer our knowledge of the symbiosis into agronomical important food crops such as maize， wheat and rice to increase nutrient and water using efficiency，with the aim of boosting the food supply for future generations. Recentlythe frameworks ofnutrient exchange and regulation between host plant and arbuscular mycorrhizal fungi orrhizobia have recently been established. I will talk about our recent progresses on signal perception and nutrient exchange in plant-microbe symbioses.

Carboranes are a class of polyhedral carbon-boron molecular clusters featuring three-dimensional aromaticity which are often viewed as 3-D analogs to benzene.They constitute a class of structurally unique molecules with exceptional thermal and chemical stabilities and the ability to hold various substituents. These properties have made them useful building blocks in the supramolecular design， medicine， catalysts and materials. However their unique structures make derivatization difficult resulting in the limited application scope. Thus，it is important and necessary to develop new methodologies for the selective functionalization of carboranes. In this lecture，I will discuss our strategies for the selective functionalization of o-carboranes at cage carbon or boron vertex and the applications of the resultant functionalized carboranes in catalysis， materials and medicine by giving examples.V
将白光滋光聚焦照射不同液体，可以形成不同形状的彩色干涉环，印相千彩虹”，这种现象涉及光学、热学、力学和声学等多种物理效应。激光加热改变了水里的温度分布，也就改变了各处的折射率，在局部形成了一个非球面的凹透镜，使得使不同波长的光各自发生干涉，以很大范围的角度出射。这里我们汇报最近几年工作中关手实验现象、物理模型以及数值模拟的结果，包括液体对流和激光波前曲率对相平彩虹的形状和形成过程的影响。相干彩虹的产生机制是非常普适的，在很多液体中都可以观察到这种现象。
1.Iterleukin-33 (IL-33） plays pleiotropic functions in maintaining tissue homeostasis in health and disease， by regulating group 2 innate lymphoid cells (ILC2s) regulatory T cells (Tregs）and other immune cells via its receptor， ST2. However it is unclear how IL-33 affects tumor immune microenvironment. We found that IL-33 inhibited the growth of orthotopic melanoma （B16-F10） in C57BL/6 mice and heterotopic breast cancer (4T1） in BALB/c mice. With flow cytometry scRNA-Seq and bioinformatics analysis， we demonstrated that IL-33 profoundly increased the proportions of infiltrating ILC2s， eosinophils and ST2+ Tregs in tumors. Mechanistically， IL-33 augmented the MHC-I expression by ILC2s and enhanced their capacity for antigen presentation. Lastly the inhibitory effect of IL-33 on tumor growth was partially dependent on Treg ST2 expression. These findings suggest that IL-33 inhibits tumor growth by regulating their immune microenvironment.2.Lung cancer is the most frequently diagnosed cancer and the leading cause of cancer-associated death worldwide. GGH CGamma-Glutamyl Hydrolase） is a lysosomal glycoprotein which affects the intracellular concentration ofpolyglutamylated folic acid by catalyzing the hydrolysis of polyglutamylated folate into transportable monoglutamate， but its oncogenic roles and underlying molecular mechanisms have not been fully studied in lung cancer. Here we found that GGH was highly expressed in tumors and significantly related to poor survival in patients with lung adenocarcinomas.Upon GGH knockdown. the cell proliferation migration and invasion were significantly decreased in lung cancer cells. Importantlyy we found that the cell autophagy was induced upon GGH silencing Mechanistically GGH regulates the autophagy may through p-AMPK-p-ULK1-BECNI signaling.In contrast of GGH， the folylpolyglutamate synthetase enzyme CFPGS） has an opposite effects on the expression of autophagy-associated proteins. Further， we observed that Cl6-ceramide was increased after GGH siRNAS treatment.In addition to those， previous study has indicated C16-ceramide can promote the autophagy in cancer cells. We speculate that GGH inhibits autophagy may through reduce folate stress and inhibit production of Cl6-ceramide， then activating p-AMPK-p-ULKI-BECNI signaling. Taken together our study suggested that GGH may not only have a prognostic markers but also play a critical role in lung cancer progression including autophagy regulation. Intervention with targeting GGH and its signaling may have translational potential for precision therapy for lung cancer.
孙汉杰先生，现任中国平安人寿保险股份有限公司总经理助理，总精算师，分管平安人寿产品中心。具有超过22年的保险行业工作经验曾任平安集团财务企划中心企划部精算室经理平安集团财务企划中心企划部副总经理；先后在产品开发、价值评估、准备金评估、企划经营等多个岗位工作过。孙汉杰先生是北美精算师正会员，也是2022年度的SOA中国委员会主席。同时，孙汉杰先生日前还担任中国银保监会人身保险业责任准备金评估利率专家咨询委员会委员。
干早、高盐、冷等不良环境等造成细胞的渗透助迫：引发生长抑制并严重影响作物的产量。细胞渗透势（膨压）变化还是植物细胞生（伸）长的动力。植物对渗透势变化的感受和响应与作物生长与抗性这两个重要农艺性状密切相关，但其详细的分子机制并不清楚。近年来，通过高精度磷酸化蛋白组学、单细胞（类群）蛋白组学等方法，以技术创新驱动科学发现，我们系统解析了高等植物RAF-SnRK2级联途径。发现受渗透助道远速透导的RAF蛋白微静是植物渗透时追感受和信号转导途径的核心组分，RAF通过磷酸化SnRK2蛋白激酶，参与了渗透胁迫和ABA对于气孔关闭、基因表达等胁迫应答过程的调节等。我们正在解析RAF蛋白激酶的上游信号途径，解析植物如何感受和应答渗透胁迫、调控植物生长的分子机制，并期望打破植物生长发育与胁迫应答的平衡，提高植（作）物对环境胁迫的适应能力。
Nutrients and energy have emerged as central modulators of developmental programs in plants and animals.The evolutionarily consened target of rapamycin (TOR）kinase is a master integrator of nutrient and energy signalling that controls growth. Despite its key regulatory roles in translation proliferation，metabolism，and autophagylittleis known about how TOR shapes developmental transitions and differentiation We show that glucose-activated TOR kinase controls genome wide histone H3 trimethylation at K27（H3K27me3） Arabidopsis thaliana，which regulates cell fate and development. We identify FERTILIZATION-INDEPENDENT ENDOSPERM （FIE）anindispensable component of Polycomb repressive complex 2 （PRC2），which catalyzes H3K27me3，asaTOR target，Direct phosphorylation by TOR promotes the dynamic translocation ofFIE from the cytoplasm to the nucleus.Mutation of the phosphorylation site on FIE abrogates the global H3K27me3 landscape， reprograms the transcriptome and disrupts organogenesis in plants，Moreover，glucose-TOR-FIE-PRC2 signalling modulates vernalization-induced floral transition. We propose that this signalling axis servesasa nutritional checkpoint leading to epigenetic silencing of key transcription factor genes that specify stem cell destiny in shoot and root meristems and control leaf，flower and silique patterning， branching， and vegetative-to-reproduction transition. Our findings reveal a fundamental mechanism of nutrient signaling in direct epigenome reprogramming， with broad relevance for the developmental control of multicellular organisms.
光和物质相互作用是支配当代社会信息、能源、环境、医学、国防军事等领域诸多科学技术的重要物理过程。在微纳尺度泳入研究光和物质相互作用物理以及光场传输、电磁场演化的精细规律，探索微纳尺度和原子水平上电磁场演化行为是否精确地满足传统连续介质麦克斯书方程组，如果不是，能否构建更加精确的理论体系，对于电磁学、光学、电动力学，乃至整个物理学都有重大的基础价值。另外，构建宏观、介观与微观相协调、经典与量子相统一的光和物质相互作用理论体系和计算方法，有望为解决单分子检测、传感、识别和成像，纳米及原子尺度显微成像等重大应用问题提供解决方案。本报告将介绍团队近年在三个前沿基础科学问题上的研究进展，包括等离激元增强的拉受散射统一理论的建筑，等离激元纳腔-分子强耦合体系光谱裂背后物理机制的探讨，以及沟通微观和宏观光学的原子水平电磁场理论的构建等，重点探究如何综合运用纳米光子学的基本概念、方法和技术等，寻找解决基础科学若干重大问题的方案。
Understanding quanturm noise is a major challenge for scaling up guantum computing systems . Despite recent developments of quantum benchmarking methods that characterize noisy quantum gates. the fundamental question of what information about noise is self-consistently learnable has been unclear even for a single CNOT gate. Here，we give a precise characterization about the learnability or Pauli noise associated with Clifford gates using graph theoretical tools，Showing the learnable information corresponds exactly to the cycle space of the pattern transfer graph of the gate set. We experimentally demonstrate Pauli noise characterization of IBM's CNOT gate，where we learn all 14 learhable degrees of freedom and bound the 2 unlearnable degrees of freedom using physical constraints: We also discuss information-theoretical lower baunds on the sample complexity of Pauli noise estimation and the possibility of using ancilla-assisted schemes to overcome these barriers.
王立新，现任广东省水利厅党组书记、厅长，曾任深圳市副市长。清华大学工学博士，在水利、环保、城市规划方面有较深造，曾长期从事政府科技、工业、贸易、社会管理等领域工作。
内存破坏漏洞是应用和系统软件中最常见的漏洞类型之一，攻击者围绕着该种漏洞所发动的一系列内存破坏攻击，给计算机系统带来了巨大的安全威助。攻击者不仅可以利用内存破坏攻击泄露目标系统的私密数据，还可以算改敏感数据实现控制流动持、内核提权等效果，进而获得自标系统的控制权。隔离保护这些私密和敏感的关键数据是阻断这类攻击的一个有效手段。由于更小的可信计算基和更低的性能损失，部署软硬协同的隔离机制是目前主流的技术路线—研究人员采用X86处理器提供的VMFUNC、MPK和MPX等硬件特性实现一系列应用场景的数据保护。然而，我们的研究发现，有些关键数据的访问通常是极其频繁的，现有软硬协同隔离机制在保护这些数据时会引入非常大的性能开销。为此，我们通过巧用和改造其他硬件特性（例如，SMAP和CET），实现更加高效的内存隔离。
We will discuss some recent results on the fractal geometry of the Markov and Lagrange spectra，which are classical objects from the theory of Diophantine approximations，and their set difference. In particular，we discuss recent results in collaboration with Erazo，Gutierrez-Romoand Romafa，which give precise asymptotic estimates for the fractal dimensions of the Markov and Lagrange spectra near3（their smaller accumulation point）and other recent collaborations with Jeffreys，Matheus，Pollicott and Vytnova，in which we prove that the Hausdorff dimension of the complement ofthe Lagrange spectrum in the Markov spectrum has Hausdorff dimension between0.594179and0.796445 We will relate these results to symbolic dynamics，continued fractions and to the study of the fractal geometry of arithmetic sums of regular Cantor sets，a subject also important for the study of homoclinic bifurcations in Dynamical Systems.
造血干细胞发育异常会导致多种血液病，如骨髓衰竭和白血病等，严重威助人类健康。细胞因子信号通路和蛋白质内稳态（proteostasis）是维持造血干细胞数量和再生功能的两个重要因素。吕考升博士综合运用分子细胞生物学、干细胞生物学和血液病学技术并结合小鼠骨髓移植和体外干细胞培养等方法，揭示了蛋白质泛素化和棕榈酰化修饰调控细胞因子信号通路的新机制并为慢性粒细胞白血病（CMML）和急性系白血病（AML）的临床治疗提供了新方案。此外，闸明了蛋白质泛素化调控核糖体组装和蛋白质翻译的新途径，发现了治疗Shwachman-Diamondsyndrome亚型骨髓衰竭综合征的新靶点。
In the past several decades，internationalisation，which is featured by people and ideas' unparalleled transnational mobility. has become a key discourse in higher education. Despite the spectacular outcomes that higher education internationalisation has achieved ， scholars have detected weaknesses and vulnerabiities in its current policy and practice，which the COVID-19 pandemic have intensified. This presentation provides a critical reflection on the field’s evo  lution and the prospects for its future， highlighting the urgent demand for concept and practice's innovation on university internationalisation at the regional，national，and institutional levets in response to the changing global field in the post-pandemic era.在过去的几十年里，以人员和思想跨国流动为特证的国际化，已经成为高等教育领域的一个重要议题。尽管高等教育国际化取得了令人喝目的成果，但学者们发现目前的国际化政和实践仍存在一些弱点和漏洞，而COVID-19的大流行加剧了这鉴弱点。新冠疫情在世界国内的流行便得全球政治、经济及文化环境发生阶段性的改变，高校若继获其国际化发展就必须对新环境做出回应与改变。该报告以西蒙马金森所提出的全球高等教育场域理论为意架，对现有文献进行了系统性和批判性的梳理，井结合对来自世界不同地区的20位高等教育国际化领域的知名资深学者的深度访谈，建构高等教育国际化这一概念的内通，并对其的高变发展和未来前最进行了批判性的反思。该报告分析了新冠疫情所导致的全球形势变化，展现了后疫情时期不同地区高等教育国际化所呈现出的新超势及重要议题。该报告同时强了在区域、国家和机构层面对高等教育国际化概念和实践创新的追切需求，并为高等教育国际化的持续发展和繁荣提供了有洞见性及可行性的战略意见。
目前的大数据处理主要都围绕大数据的volume和vclocity这两个挑战，对于variety挑战的研究相对较少。通用的数据处理技术因其广泛的适用性和相对低的平均开发维护成本，一直受到商业数据库管理系统的青睐。大数据泛构（big data genhierarchy）把数据抽象成度量空间中的点，仅利用数据间距离的三角不等性进行数据的管理和挖掘等工作，具有高度的通用性，有望成为下一代通用数据处理系统的重要组件。
人类疾病的发生发展与蛋白质表达和功能的异常密切相关，而蛋白的表达和功能受基因表达、翻译后修饰等多重因素的调控。因而，单维度的基因组学、转录组学、蛋白质组学很难全面解析疾病的发病机制及关键靴标。基于此，曹丽伟综合利用包括蛋白组、磷酸蛋白组、糖基化蛋白组、基因组、转录组的蛋白基因组学来分析膜腺痘临床样本，解析了膜腺痘的痘症生物学，并促进鉴定到潜在膜腺癌早期诊断标及治疗記点。此外，为了鉴定高度糖基化的文滋病表面膜蛋日的糖基化状态，曹丽伟百次建立了基于EndoH和PNGaseF的连续酶切法，该方法能够全面鉴定艾滋病包膜糖蛋白的糖基化状态，为艾滋病疫苗生产提供标准糖基化图谱。
氮化铁（GaN）是最重要的宽禁带半导体之，已经广泛地应用在短波长发光二极管和激光器上也将是下一代高频、高功率和高温电子器件的关键半导体材料。由于具有很高的迁移率、饱和速度和二维电子气密度，AIGaN/GaN异质结构被认为是发展高性能电力电子器件、微波毫米波器件和单片电路的理想材料。本报告将对宽禁带半导体以及本团队在氮化镍电子器件的研究活动和成果作简要介绍。本报告首先针对正在兴起的微波无线电力传输技术的低功率微波整流电路，设计和制造了准垂直结构的GaN肖特基二极管。采用重参杂外延层和图形化的肖特基阳极，降低了GaNSBD的串联电阻。对于反向击穿电压50V的器件，开启电阻为1.459，结电容为0.87pF。设计并测试了微波整流电路。源于优秀的二极管器件性能和微波电路设计，在工作频率905MHz和输入功率23dBm的条件下，转换效率达到92%。在2.45GHz和输入功率25dBm的条件下，转换效率达到91%。在905MHz工作频率下，完成了传输距离3米的实验，发射和接收功率分别为39dBm和12.5dBm。另外，本报告也将对GaN射频场效应晶体管和GaN功率开关器件的研究做介绍。
Quantum phase estimation is a crucial component in quantum algorithms which are believed to achieve an exponential speedup over their classical counterparts for solving problems，such as integer factorization，the Hamiltonian spectrum. However， the conventional phase estimation algorithm which is based on ihe quantum Fourier transfoFm， reguites ancillary qubits to perform the controlled unitary operators and quantum error correction to combat noise.These requirements surpass the capability of the current noisy intermediate-scale quantum(NISQ) dlevices.The control-free phase estimation is an appealing variant in the NISQ era，where the unitary of interest is repeatedly applied instead of its control version.in this work，we develop an error mitigation method for the control-free phase estimation.We prove a theorem that under the first-order correction， the noise channels with only Hermitian Kraus operators do not ohange the phases of a unitary operator，and therefore，the benign types of noise for phase estimation are identified. By using the randomized compiling protocol，we can convert the genericnoise in the phase estimation circuits into stochastic Pauli noise，which setisfies the condlition of our theorem:Thus we achieve a noise-resilient phase estimation without any guantum resource overhead.The simulated experimenis show that our method.can significahtly reduce the estimation error of ihe phases by up to twvo orders.of magnitude.Our method paves the way for the utilization of quantum phase estimation before the advent or fault-tolerant guantum computers.
随着传感器、人工智能理论和技术的飞速发展，机器人的灵巧操作已得到国内外高度关注，它在精密制造、科学实验、助老助残与医疗服务等重要领域都有追切需求，被Science评为机器人领域最具挑战问题之一。2018年我国科技日报将机器人灵巧操作中的“触觉传感器”和“机器人核心算法”重要两个方面纳入了“卡脖子技术”，因此机器人灵巧操作技术也被我国列入新一代人工智能国家发展战略的重要内容。报告围绕机器人灵巧操作的“触觉感知与交互学习”展开，首先闸述了机器人灵巧操作的发展和背景，接着详细介绍了操作触觉感知的研究工作，然后介绍了人机自然交互操作的方法，进一步针对开发的新型灵巧未端闻述了机器人抓取操作学习方法，最后总结展望了机器人灵巧操作的发展趋势。
1.Osteoporosis (OP)，a disease that weakens bones， affects more than 200 million people around the world， and above 70% ofpatients are over 65 years old. PTHis an approved drug of severe OP to stimulate bone formation. However elderly patients do not respond to PTH treatment as well as young ones.The mechanism that leads to this difference is still unknown.In this study，we found that Tumor Necrosis Factor alpha (TNF-a）， an up-regulated potent cytokine inelderly OP patients， can suppress PTH induced cAMP production and CREB phosphorylation in osteocytes in vitro. In addition. the global TNFRI and TNFR2 knockout （dKO） mice Sshowed a higher bone volume CBV） and bone mineral density (BMD） compared to their wild-type littermates after intermittent PTH administration. suggesting that PTH-driven bone formation could be inhibited by upregulated TNF-a signaling pathway. Furthermore， we found that TNF receptor-associated factor 2 (TRAF2），an important molecule downstream of TNF-a signaling，interacts with and promotes Gas ubiguitination.resulting in restraining PTH induction of CREB phosphorylation. Taken together our results suggest that through a TRAF2-dependent manner the TNF-a signaling pathway could be an important potential target for improving the effectiveness ofPTH treatment in elderly OP patients.2.Genetic alterations of cancer cells can shape the tumor-promoting microenvironment.Kriippel-like factor 5 （KLF5）， located at the second most frequently deleted chromosomal region of human prostate cancer CPCa）， has been reported to modulate tumor progression and the secretion of inflammatory cytokines. However the role of KLFS in PCa microenvironment is unclear. Here， we demonstrate that KLF5 plays a crucial role in reprogramming PCa microenvironment by modulating tumor-associated macrophages (TAMs）. In Pten-null mouse prostates， KIf5 knockout significantly increases the infiltration of TAMs. KIf5 deletion upregulates multiple factors associated with TAMs recruitment and polarization. Including MIF， Sppl， CXCL1， and CCL2.CD74， the receptor of MIF，is associated with macrophageinfiltration in PCa. Consistently， MIF is negatively correlated with KLF5 expression both in mRNA and protein level. ISO-l，an inhibitor of MIF，inhibits macrophage accumulation and decreased the ratio of CD206* M2 macrophage in total macrophage in K7/5-loss tumors.Suppression of TAMs accumulation by PLX3397， an inhibitor of CSFIRy and ISO-1 relieved K1f5 deficiency-induced prostate tumor growth and angiogenesis respectively.This study unveils a novel KLF5-dependent mechanism in M2 macrophage infiltration in the microenvironment of PCa， providing implications for the development of novel prognostic and mmunologicallytherapeutic targets.
Human ATP-binding cassette (ABC)subfamily A(ABCA）transporters mediate the transport of various lipid compounds across the membrane. Mutations in human ABCA transporters have been described to cause severe hereditary disorders associated with impaired lipid transport. Here，we present three cryO-EM structures of human ABCA4，aretina-specific lipid importer，and two cryO-EM structures of human ABCA3，a lung-specific lipid exporter，in distinct functional states atresolutions of 3.3-3.4 A.In the nucleotide-free state，the two transmembrane domains（TMDs） of ABCA4 and ABCA3 exhibit alateral-opening'conformation，allowing the lateral entry of substrate from both leaflets of the lipid bilayer.In the ATP-bound state，the two TMDS of ABCA4 and ABCA3 display a closed conformation， which precludes substrate binding， Our results help rationalize the disease-causing mutations in human ABCA4 and ABCA3 and suggest a conserved  ' lateral access and extrusion' mechanism for both lipid export and import mediated by ABCA transporters.
The ongoing revolution of cryo-EM has enabled novel approaches for obtaining deep insights into highly dynamic protein machines. Through our cryo-EM studies of several ABC transporters that perform different functions，we have uncovered how distinct tasks of substrate translocation are accomplished by the unique actions of these transporters Importantly，our own research experience in the past decade is an excellent demonstration of how cryo-EM methodology and the mechanistic study of ABC transporters stimulate each other's development，thus emphasizing the extremely versatile nature and yet-to-be-realizedpotentialof cryo-EM in biological research.

Quantum states of light opens up a new avenue for spectroscopy by utilizing the parameters，i.e，entanglement， squeezing and photon statistics. Imaging and controlling the electron and vibrational dynamics of molecules can be achieved， towards unprecedented resolution and precision， not accessible by classical laser pulses. An overview of our recent work on quantum-light spectroscopic probes of ultrafast electron dynamics will be presented， including multidimensional coherent probe， photon-coincidence counting and Raman spectra. Microscopic models for quantum dynamics will be further discussed. 
在信息时代，密码学是保障信息安全的核心技术和基础支撑。隐私计算在数字经济中至关重要，是保护隐私条件下实现数据价值的关键技术。在本次报告中，我们将介绍密码学的历史，以及相关前沿研究，概述与隐私计算相关的密码学技术。

With the advance in sensors ，data become ubiguitous. To make sense of the data we have to solve higher and higher dimensional problems that would seem intractable to solve. However many high-dimensional probfems have solutions that live in low-dimensional spaces. Sparsity is a way to exploit the low-dimensional structure of solutions to obtain feasible solution methods for high-dimensional problems. 人类基因组测序完成后，出人意料地发现编码基因的数目远小于预估，说明在RNA水平上存在多样的调控机理来提高基因组的复杂度。这种复杂度的扩展主要通过RNA可变剪接实现：超过90%的基因都有一种以上的剪接亚型，从而翻译成不同的蛋白质亚型。剪接的调控与包括癌症在内的多种人类疾病密切相关，因此对癌症中剪接异变的研究有重要的意义。近期还发现mRNA的翻译也有着复杂的调控过程，其中很多环形RNA可以通过非经典翻译过程来指导蛋白合成，因此成为扩展蛋白组复杂性的一个新机理。同时，利用RNA层面的基础知识，来研发新型的核酸或蛋白药物，使得在RNA层面对基因组进行操控成为可能。我讲对实验室近年来在RNA领域的工作，包括RNA剪接调控，翻译调控，以及利用合成生物学方法对RNA的特异性操控这三方面，做一个简单介绍。
In this talk，I privide two recent proposals for achieving quantum enhanced sensitivity in many-body probes.While the first proposal exploits the feature of the ground state for sensing.the second approach relies on the non-equilibrium dynamics.Second order quantum phase transitions，with well-known features such as long-rang entanglement， symmetry breaking，and gap closing，exhibit quantum enhancement for sensing at criticality. However， it is unclear which of these features are responsible for this onhancement. To address this issue， we investigate phase transitions in free-formionic topological systems that exhibit neither symmetry-breaking nor long-range. We using topological edge states near the phase boundary. Remarkably ，such accessible in solid state experiments. We illustrate the results with ID Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain and a 2D Chern insulator which are both experimentally accessible. While neither symmetry-breaking nor long-range entanglement are essential， gap closing remains as the major candidate for the ultimate source of quantum enhanced sensing. In addition， we show that the dynamics of a many-body system can also be this method， one can use sequential measurements on a single qubit of a many-body probe with intervals of free evolution. We show that by increasing the length of the sequence one can enhance the precision well-beyond the standard limit accessible to classical sensors.
With the advance in sensors，data become ubiquitous.To make sense of the data we have to solve higher and higher dimensional problems that would seem intractable to solve.However，many high-dimensional problems have solutions that live in low-dimensional spaces.Sparsity is a way to exploit the low-dimensional structure of solutions to obtain feasible solution methods for high-dimensional problems.Here in this talk，l will introduce regularization methods that enforce sparsity in solutions and their applications to several image reconstruction problems including single-molecule localization microscopy and ground-based astronomy.

二维（2D）材料家族包涵了多种类型的层状材料，它的层状薄膜可以具有原子级的厚度，以及独特奇异的电学、光学以及其他特性。在过去十多年里，人们在二维材料和器件方面取得了多项重要进展，这为其从可见光到红外以及太赫兹（THz）波段范围内的光电应用提供了广阔的前景。在本次报告中，我将首先简要回顾二维材料中光与物质相互作用的若干进展，特别是若干极化激元。尔后我将重点讨论与光电子相关的几个主题。为了获得由通常大约几纳米有限长度的光与物质相互作用构建的高性能器件，我们尝试了光电器件的新设计和制备方法，实现了从可见光到红外传感和太赫兹光波段的调制。我将通过几个示例展示石墨烯、二硫化钥和二确化鸽，及其相关异质结构和/或混合架构方面的研究进展。最后将展望二维材料在柔性光电子器件方面的发展前景。

Intelligent Reflecting Surface （IRS）is adigitally controlled metasurface that can be densely deployed in wireless networks to reconfigure the propagation channels among wireless nodes by dynamically tuning the signal reflection.IRS is able to not only significantly improve the networkspectral and energy eficiency for communications，but also greatly enhance the performance forother emerging applications such as wireless power transfer，sensing and localization，etc. The existing research on IRS has mainly considered wireless systems with single-lRS-reflections atthelink level，which does not reveal the full potential of IRS forfuture wireless networks.In this talk，we will focus on the main design challenges in efficiently integrating IRS to wireless networks，including IRS reflection optimization，channel acquisition and optimal deployment，withan emphasis on double-/multi-iRS-reflections.Furthermore，we will present emerging new architectures of IRS and their advantages for future applications.We will conclude the talk bydiscussing research directions worthy of further investigation in the future.
Entanglement detection isessentialin quantum inforimation science and guantium many-body physics. li has been proved that entanglement exists almost surely fora random gurantum state，while the realizations of effective entanglement criteria usually consume exponential resources，and efficient criteria often perform poorly without prior knowledge.This fact implies afundamenial limitation might exdist in the deiectabfiity of enianglement:In thiswork，we formalize ihis limitation asa fiuindamental tirade-off between the efficiency and effeotiveness of enianglement criteria via a systematic method totheoretically evaluate the detection capability of entanglement criteria.For asystem couoled to an environmentwe prove that any entanglement criterion needs exponentially. many observables to detect the entanglement effectively when restricted tosingle-copy operations.Otherwise，the detection capability ofthe criterion will decay double-exponentially. Furthermore，if multi-copy joint measurements are allowed，the effectiveness of entanglement detection can be exponentially improved，which implies a quantum advantage in entanglement detection problems.

OTFS has drawn great interest in the past five years， as a modulation method that is robust to temporal channel variations， as well as allows efficient implement of various MIMO schemes.One interpretation of OTFS is as modulation in the delay-Doppler-angle domain.This naturally raises the question about available measurement results and models for propagation channels in this multi-dimensional space. Consequently， this talk will start out with a review of the fundamentals of OTFS， in particular its interpretation as modulating the delay-Doppler domain， followed by a discussion of channel sounding techniques and measurement results for delay-Doppler-angle channels. Discussions about the capability of OTFS to effectively estimate those channels will wrap up this talk.
Silicon-based devices have served the semiconductor industry for more than 60 years. The device performances are approaching the fundamental material limits. Now is the time to reshape the topic of electronic devices using more advanced semiconductors. Wide bandgap semiconductors， such as gallium nitride (GaN) and silicon carbide (SiC)， have higher electron velocity， higher breakdown electric field strength， and higher operating temperature limit， all of which make them promising candidates in the upcoming era of greener electronics. In the past 20 years， GaN has shown excellent performances in solid-state lighting， RF and power devices.Since 2013， both governments and industry have invested heavily in vertical GaN techniques， making new device architectures and processes available. Most notably， GaN avalanche devices are being developed， which show great potential in power switches and single- photon detectors. In this talk， I will review my research work on impact ionization and avalanche in GaN devices for power， photonics， and RF applications.
 Large classes of the general-purpose optimisation algorithms at the heart of modern artificial intelligence and machine learning technologies are inspired by models of Darwinian evolution. In this talk we show how the foundational computational complexity analysis of such algorithms leads to an understanding of their behaviour and performance. Such understanding in turn allows informed decisions on how to set the many parameters and how to improve the algorithms to allow for the obtainment of better solutions in shorter time. We provide three concrete examples of how such analyses can lead to counter intuitive insights into how to design sexual evolution inspired algorithms (using populations and recombination) and how to set their parameters such that they can considerably outperform their single trajectory and mutation only (asexual) counterparts at 1) hillclimbing unimodal functions， at 2) escaping local optima， and at 3) general global optimisation of multimodal functions. For such performance to be achieved the required algorithmic setups are considerably different from those traditionally recommended， and sometimes particularly surprising， hence unlikely to be tested in empirical analyses. We conclude the talk by presenting experimental results that confirm the superiority of the designed algorithms that was proven for benchmark functions with significant structures， for classical combinatorial optimisation problems with practical applications.

Geobiology explores the relationship between life and the physical Earth. Geobiology encompasses field and laboratory experiments designed to understand how interacting biological and physical processes shape environments， both locally and globally， as well as geological investigations of how Earth and life have interacted across our planet's entire 4.6-billion-year history.

飞秒激光加工作为微纳制造的一种新方法，具有材料适用性广、分辨率高、热影响小的优势，广泛用于制造多种具有复杂三维结构的光电器件。其原理主要是基于焦点处的超快激光脉冲与写入材料的非线性相互作用，从而引起加工材料在局部产生永久的结构变化，可以在大部分透明材料中产生具有微纳米尺寸的光学结构。

This paper explores howconsumers detect real and fake reviews in online word-of-mouth. Drawing on the truth-default theory that emerged from the lie detection literature in the recent decade， we propose that consumers have a general tendency to believe a review to be true more than fake (i.e.， the truth bias)， and that this tendency is greater for negative reviews than positive reviews.
We study the long run effects of immigration on US political ideology. We establish a new result: historical European immigration is associated with stronger preferences for redistribution and a more liberal ideology among Americans today.

Acoustic wave resonators are very sensitive to the adsorption of external mass on their surfaces. which makes them promising for molecular sensing. However， they face significant challenges including poor selectivity as gas sensors and strong in-liquid attenuation as biosensors. This talk will introduce novel designs for addressing the limitations of acoustic-resonator-based molecular sensors. The first part of the talk will focus on solving the poor selectivity issue of conventiona gas sensors by exploiting dual transduction mechanisms based on film bulk acoustic wave resonator (FBAR) and surface acoustic wave (SAW) resonators.

人类历史上曾经有那么多思想家提出理想社会的范本，孔子讲大同社会，孟子讲老吾老以及人之老，佛陀讲众生平等，耶稣讲天堂如何如何。但是，却没有一个古代社会能够让绝大多数普通人吃饱肚子。人类是到了化肥和育种技术发明后，才有能力解决大部分人的温饱问题的。现代社会与古典社会的根本区别，在于现代社会孕育了一种“知识炼金术”的力量。这股力量能够帮助人们超脱以暴力互相伤害的困境，创造维护文明与繁荣的正增长社会条件。但是，这股力量本身并不是自然而然发生的，也不会在前进的历程上一帆风顺。如果技术力量不加控制，将会对人类社会产生重大的不可逆转的影响。一些逆转已经发生，另一些逆转正在路上。本讲座将带领大家回顾科技史上的重大时刻、技术与启蒙之间的密切关系，并审视现代社会在当下如何受到技术和政治力量合流的多重挑战。

In this talk， I introduce a new semi-parametric modeling method for heterogeneous treatment effect estimation and individualized treatment selection using a covariate-specific treatment effect (CSTE) curve with high-dimensional covariates. The proposed method is quite flexible to depict both local and global associations between the treatment and baseline covariates， and thus is robust against model mis-specification in the presence of high-dimensional covariates.

Pyrethrum (Tanacetum cinerarifolium) is a daisy-like plant from Asteracease family that well-known for synthesis of natural pesticide named pyrethrins in its flower. Although the dried plant and extract have been used for more than one thousand years， the pathway of their biosynthesis in Planta was not quite clear. There are six types of pyrethrins， esters constituted by one of two acid moieties (chrysanthemic acid - type I and pyrethric acid - type I) combines with one of three alcohol moieties (jasmolone pyrethrolone and cinerolone， corresponding to jasmolin， pyrethrin and cinerin respectively).

动力降尺度作为衔接全球和区域气候、污染模式的有效方法，存在一定的不确定性。报告首先以初始场、边界场和云参数化方案选择为例，阐释动力降尺度过程中降水及臭氧模拟的不确定性。进而，基于高分辨率全球气候模式(25km大气、10km海洋)和传统CMIP5模式，探讨高精度全球模式对海洋热浪模拟能力的改进。最后，在极端天气事件(如高温热浪、静稳)频发的背景下，揭示气候变化下复合极端天气及不同污染源排放情景对臭氧和PM2.5污染可能的非线性影响。

Machine learning has become increasingly popular nowadays. It has been applied in a variety of fields， such as artificial intelligence， translation， system management， robotics， logistics， as well as education. When machines can be responsible for many more jobs traditionally operated by human-beings， many interesting questions pop up. How do machines learn? How do people learn? 机器学习是目前最令人瞩目的新技术之一。被应用于各种领域和场景，例如人工智能，翻译，系统管理，机器人，物流，以及教育。当机器的学习能力越来越惊人，逐渐可以取代越来越多的人类工作，我们开始思考一些有意思的问题：比如机器到底是如何学习的？而人类是如何学习的？在21世纪的今天，我们需要什么样的学习方式来获得改造世界的重要能力，如创造力，合作力，批判性思考能力，以及交流能力？这次沙龙将从学习科学和教育技术的角度带领大家去探讨这些关于机器和人类学习的有趣问题。

储能电池的高倍率充放电性能是电动汽车广泛推广的拦路虎之一。汽车在启动和爬坡时电动机需要较大电流(大倍率放电) ，汽车运行中充电时间要求尽量短(大倍率充电) 。而当前锂离子电池的现状是充电耗时久，导致充电难，以及高倍率放电导致电池寿命快速衰减，甚至有可能发生安全问题。
